nara śreṣṭhaḥ prabrūyāt dharma tatparaḥ harma niṣṭhaḥ kṛtaḥ rājā tad prāmāṇyāt bhayena vā dharmataḥ satatam rājā a prajā dharmeṇa pālayet nyāyena pālyamānāḥ tu rājñaḥ dhyāyanti vaiśubham ṣaṣṭha maṃśam labhet rājā ubhayayoḥ puṇya pāpayoḥ kṛte yuge bhavet rājā tretāyām dvāpare kalau prajā pīḍana saṃtāpāt samudbhūta uḍatā śanaḥ rājyam śriyam kulam prāṇān a dagdhvā an nivartate dharma śīle nṛpe yasmāt sarva loka anukampayā dharma mārga avatārāya vedaḥ aṣṭa aṅgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ tyā śāstra vādena kāma artha abhiratān nṛpān śanais dharme niyuṃjīta jñātvā yogam punar kramāt tat tat saṃsāra paṅka nirmanam kaḥ tena sadṛśaḥ pitā mṛtena nṛpati nirvāpayati yaḥ śanais ajñāna vanhi saṃtaptam kaḥ tam na pratipūjayet muni varaiḥ śāntaiḥ bhāṣitam yat su śobha naṃ vai avidyā rāga vākyena mṛdunā alalitena ca tena api kim tena saṃsāraiḥ gati hetunā yat śrutvā jāyate puṇyam rāga ādīnām ca saṃkṣayaḥ purāṇam bhāratam vedāḥ śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca munibhiḥ supraṇītā niśrūyate dharma hetunā putra dāra ādi saṃsāraḥ puṃsām uktaḥ tu bandhanam sat yoga abhyāsa kāraṇam idam jñeyam idam jñeyam yaḥ sarva jñātum icchati api varṣa sahasra āyuḥśāstra antam na adhigacchati mā svam jīvitam laghu vijñāya akṣara tad mātre pāralaukikam ācaret yaḥ puṇya bhāram uddoḍhum aśaktaḥ pāralaukikam bhitaḥ upi saḥ mūrkhaḥ syāt śakti yuktaḥ api aśaktikaḥ saṃsāra stham svam ātmānam uttārayitum akṣamaḥ sa paṇḍitaḥ sa śaktaḥ syāt saḥ tapasvī jita iṃdriyaḥ yaḥ śiva jñāna sadbhāvam ālocayitum udyataḥ yaḥ pradadyāt mahīm kṛtsnām mahā meruṃcakāñcanam yaḥ śṛṇoti śiva jñānam nyāyāt tat vavīti nitya naimittikam kāmyam trividham liṅga pūjanam tat tvā aham saṃpravakṣyāmi śiva tuṣṭi karam param atha go deha saṃbhūtaiḥ paḍaṅga vidhinā śivaḥ nityam saṃpūjitaḥ śīghram narāṇām saṃprasīdati sura asuraiḥ mathyamāne kṣīrodāt sāgara uttamāt pañca gāvaḥ samutpannāḥ sarva lokasya mātaraḥ nandā bhadrā suśīlā ca surabhiḥ sumanāḥ tathā dade pañca gāvaḥ muni śreṣṭhāḥ surabhiḥ bhūmim āgatā sarva loka upakārāya devānām tarpaṇāya ca turabhiḥ saṃsthitā bhūmau srānā śaṃkarasya ca gomayam rocanā mūtram kṣīram dadhi ghṛtam gavām ṣaṣ aṅgāni pavitrāṇi sarva siddhi karāṇi ca tatra āste padma hastā śrīḥ śrīvṛkṣaḥ tena sa smṛtaḥ bījāni utpala padmānām punar jātāni gaḥ mayāt pītā gorocanā jātā pavitrā sarvamaṅgalā go mūtrāt gugguluḥ jātaḥ devatānām su tṛptaye kṣīrāt vīryam tu sarveṣām jātam iddhi su maṅgalam ghṛta amṭa tantu saṃbhūtam amarāṇām su tṛptaye strāpya śīta ambunā paścāt candanena vilepayet pāyasam su jala āḍhyam tu dadhi yuktam ghṛta ptam māpayet anena vidhinā devaḥ ṣaḍaṅgena prasīdati bhāvāt nityam abhāvāt ca caturdaśī aṣṭamīṣu ca anena vidhinā a liṅgam yaḥ kaścid pūjayet sadā śiva bhaktaḥ samuttārya kulānām ekaviṃśatim vṛttyāḥ bhaktyāḥ bhaktyāḥ pūjayanti iha te piyānti śiva ālayam mālākāraḥ śivasya evam mahā bhaktyā supūjanāt tathivyām ekarāj bhūtvā āsa gacchet śivaiḥ mandiram tad akṣareṇa mantreṇa śivam ekāgra mānasaḥ śiva bhaktaḥ samuttārya kulānām ekaviṃśatim bhaktyā ye piprapaśyanti deva kārya niyojitāḥ prayānti svāminā sārdham śrīmat śiva puram mahat punar iha āyātaḥ bhṛtya varga samanvitaḥ bhuktvā ābhogān su vipulān pṛthivyām ekarām bhavet yeṣām pattrāṇi puṣpāṇi liṅgasya eva arcane sadā mahā gāyāḥ ca gacchanti rudra lokam na saṃśayaḥ pūjyamānam ca vidhinā ayaḥ paśyet śraddhayā aśivam tat upi yāga phalaṃkṛt saṃprāptavan na atra saṃśayaḥ modayet puṇyam īśvaram ye samādhinā bhaktyā anumodayet īśam snāna arcana kṛte tu yat śiva puṇyām aśeṣa āḍhyām aśeṣa jana sevitām śiva dharmāḥ śivena uktāḥ su sūkṣmāḥ mu mahā phalāḥ pīrtitāḥ te samāsena nitya pūjā samāśritāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām nityanaimittikapūjāvidhiḥ nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ śaṃkarasya kriyā yogam śrotum icchāmahe vayam uvāca proktam sanatkumāreṇa yayā sāya kapardinaḥ tat śṛṇudhvam jita klamāḥ uvāca pūjanam manasā a brahmacaryeṇa puṇyaiḥ vāc kāya saṃbhavaiḥ kriyāyogaḥ hi vidvobhiḥ yoginām samudāhṛtaḥ yat phalam samavāpnoti sthāṇoḥ sthānam hi kārayet harācaliṃgam evam vā kārayitvā yat aśnute kāni mālyāni ca uktāni kāni na arhati śaṃkare ke dhūpa avallabhāḥ ke ca keca varjyāḥ sadā eva hi phalam kim asti kim phalam gīta vādane śaṃkarasya hitam ca api tat aśeṣam vadasva me mad bhagavant vidhivat puṇyam tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu yaḥ tu bātyā artha saṃyogaḥ kriyā yogaḥ saḥ ucyate devālaya ādi karaṇa itat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu yaḥ tu devālayam śambhoḥ śailam dārvam atha mṛd mayam vā api śṭaṇutasya mune phalam prāpnoti tat phalam śambhoḥ yaḥ kārayati mandiram kulānām śatam āgāmi atītam ca tathā śatam kārayan śūlinā udhām anayati akṣayalaḥ śatām sapta janma kṛtam pāpam su alpam vā yat iva uca mad bhoḥ ālaya vinyāsaiḥ prārambhadevaiḥ naśyati pratiṣṭhām samavāpnoti sa naraḥ sārvalaukikām praśasta deśa bhū bhāge śivasya āyatanam tuyaḥ iṣṭakānām vinyāsaḥ yāvat varṣāṇi tiṣṭhati tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi śiva loke mahīyate māḥ kārayet śam bho liṅgam vā lakṣaṇa anvitam ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi yathākramam pratyekaśaḥ samastān adivānām pratipadyate haṃbholiṅgam pratiṣṭhāpya su praśaste niveśane puruṣaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ syāt nai tat svam maraṇam nayet ye bhaviṣyanti ye atītāḥ ā kalpāt puruṣāḥ kule tān tān tārayate sthāpya liṅgam sarva guṇa anvitam samuddhṛtya kula aṣṭakam ha kriyamāṇam tu yaḥ prekṣya cetasā yaḥ anucitayet tu saṃpadām ebhaviṣyati evam tasya kulam sadyas yāti svargeṇa saṃśayaḥ prajāpatiḥ yamaṃsthāḥ pyatama ahata va kiṃkarāḥ pāśa daṃḍa dharāḥ nityam vicariṣyati bhū tale dharma adharma anuśāstāraḥ mama avākyam niśamyatām kevalam ye jagannātham śaṃkaram samupāśritāḥ tvayā te parihartavyāḥ teṣām na asi atra saṃsthitiḥ ca māheśvara āloka itad cittāḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ te tu rudra gaṇāḥ jñeyāḥ sadā tyājyāḥ su dūratas ye tiṣṭhataḥ svapaṃtaḥ ca gacchantaḥ vaidivāniśam dūratas ye puṣpa dhūpa vāsobhiḥ bhūpaṇaiḥ śva ātma vallabhaiḥ arcayanti nate grātyāḥ nara āhara samāśrayāḥ hara ālaye parityājyāḥ tepa atri puruṣaṃkulam yena vā āyatanam śambhoḥ kāritam tad kula udbhavam puṃsām śatam na avalokyam bhavadbhiḥ duṣṭa cetasā nara ayutam tad kula jam bhavatā aṃśa āsana atigam punar vaivasvataḥ gāthā etāvai parameṣṭhinā hitāya jñāpayāmāsa dūtān prati yathātatham sthāpayitvā śubhram liṅgam samyak saṃpūjyamānavaḥ yam yam prārthayate kāmam tam tam śaṃkaraḥ toṣitaḥ mayā tīrtha udakaiḥ tathā atyarthaiḥ strānaiḥ saṃtoṣitaḥ śivaḥ tena kāntiḥ iyam jātā devebhyaḥ tu adhikāmam manas prasādaḥ saumya tvam śarīrasya ca nirvṛtiḥ yāni abhīṣṭa nivāsāṃsi yat manaḥ vāc kāya karmabhiḥ liṅgam saṃpūjayet nityam tam tam prāpnoti mānavaḥ prāpnoti abhimatān kāmān devānām api durlabhān candana aguru karpūraiḥ kuṅkuma uśīra padmakaiḥ pradattam śambhave dhūpam ādinam puṣpa abhāvāt śivaḥ pūjyaḥ bhṛṅgaiḥ dūrvā śubhaiḥ māla pattra aiśvasa dadāti aiśvarān guṇān evam yaḥ pūjayet nityam śivam parama kāraṇam sa prayāti akṣaiḥ yān lokān pūjyamānaḥ apsaras gaṇaiḥ yadā akālāt iha āyāti rājā ārājya īśvaraḥ mahān pṛthivyām ekarāḥ bhūtvā kramāt mokṣam avāpnuyāt hi bhavet bhū sugandhaiḥ śvasurāmāṃsī karpūra aguru candanaiḥ mustā ādi yukta toyena trāpayet īśvaram sadā sūkṣmaiḥ kārpāsikaiḥ sadā vāsobhiḥ pūjayet īśam anyaiḥ ca eva ātmanaḥ priyaiḥ śubhāni yāni bhakṣyāṇi bhojyāni abhimatāni ca yoginam śaṃkaram matvā aśubha ācāram dvijottamam mad avyakta rūpāya nāmnā tasmai nivedayet saṃkrāntiḥ viṣuvat yogaḥ vyatīpātaḥ ayana dvayam tathā anye tu śubhāḥ kālāḥ proktāḥ naimittikāḥ sadā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām nityanaimittikavidhikathanam nāma pūjyāḥ śiva yoginaḥ pratiśraya anna pāna enaśayyā vastra ādibhiḥ sadā yaḥ karoti hi śuśrūṣām vidhivat śiva yoginaḥ bhaktyā tasya phalam śṛṇu sūrya dīpti pratīkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ taḥ smṛtaḥ śivapuram gacchet saḥ sa nakula saṃyu taḥ kalpa koṭi śatam divyam sevyamānaḥ sa tiṣṭhati tad ante viṣṇu bhavane tāvatkālam vasat punar saṃprāpya modate punar bhogān nānāvidhān bhuktvā pṛthivyām jāyate punar kule mahati viprāṇām prajñā śīla guṇa anvitaḥ tatas sa pūrva bhāvena yogi indram samupāsate tad samparkāt śiva jñānam prāpya yogam tu sevate yogāt viraktaḥ saṃsārāt prāpnoti paramam padam tatas tatas cāndrāyaṇa ādikaḥ svādhyāyaḥ ca japaḥ proktaḥ śiva mantrasya sa tridhā dhyāna yajñaḥ samākhyātaḥ śivaiḥ cintā muhur muhur adhyāpanam adhyayanam vyākhyā śravaṇa cintane iti pañca trakāraḥ yaḥ jñāna yajñaḥ prakīrtitaḥ uttarottara vaiśiṣṭyam sarva pāṃparikīrtitam pañcānām api yajñānām jñānam dhyānam vimukti dam kriyā nāsti jñānam vinā ādhyānam nāsti jñānam ayoginaḥ jñānam dhyānam ca yasya astitīrṇaḥ tena bhava arṇavaḥ jñānam prasannam ekāgram aśeṣa apāya varjitam śruti citām ayam jñānam vikalpa bahulam yatas śrutvā vivardhayet jñānam prājñaḥ tat citayet sadā ciṃtanam niśvayāt bhāvanam tasya niṣṭhā kāle prasanna tā mahulam niḥsāram ati kaṣṭam ca bhavam bhāvayataḥ śanais iti prasannam yat jñānam bhāvanā mayam uttamam rāga ādyaiḥ aparāmṛṣṭa tat vijñeyam vimukti dam ajñāna pāśa baddha tvāt amuktaḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ tasmāt jñānena muktaḥ syāt ajñānasya parikṣayāt saṃsāra bījam ajñānam saṃsārī ajñaḥ pumān yatas manas asya niṣṭattiḥ syāt prakāśāt tamasaḥ yathā ajñāne sati rāga ādya adharma adharmau ca tad vaśau dharma adharma vaśāt puṃsām śarīram upajāyate śarīre sati saṃkleśaiḥ sarvaḥ saṃyujyate yatas tatas kleśa vyapoha artham punar deham kāmayet ajñāna vinivṛtti auca rāga ādīnām asaṃbhavaḥ rāga ādi upaśamāt puṃsām puṇya pāpa parikṣayaḥ tad kṣayāt ca śarīreṇa punar saṃyujyate nahi sarvadā eva na bādhyate tasmāt ajñāna mūlāni sarva duḥkhāni dehinām mānena ca tat ajñānam nivarteta na karmabhiḥ puṇya pāpa parikṣayaḥ mokṣa arthī puruṣaḥ tasmāt jñānam eva sadā abhyaset mṛdyamānam sadā yadvat darpaṇam nirmalam bhavet manas abhyāsāt ta thā puṃsām buddhiḥ bhavati nirmalā jñāna amṛta rasaḥ yena na āsvāditaḥ bhavet ca jñāna amṭata rasaḥ prāyas yena na āsvāditaḥ bhavet tṛptasya kṛtakṛtyasya yoginaḥ syāt saṃpūrṇaḥ priya darśanaḥ na asti jñānāt param kiṃcid pavitram pāpa nāśanam saṃnyāsa tīrtha āśrama karma yogāḥ svarga artham etat punar eti martyaḥ jñānam dhuvaṃśa anti karam mahā artham nityam paṭheyaḥ niyataḥ mahātmā tathā ekacittaḥ satatam śṛṇoti paurāṇa dharma munibhiḥ praṇītam pāpa kṣayāt tasya bhavet vimuktiḥ dānena vividhān bhogān jñānāt mokṣam avāpnuyāt ha asinā a chitvā avidehaḥ śivam ṛcchati bhavet vandhaḥ śubhena vā muktiḥ katham teṣām nivaddhānām śubha aśubhaiḥ nahi dehabhṛtā aśakyam karma tyaktum śubha aśubham tyāgāt adharma śva saṃtiṣṭhet niścalaḥ katham tasmāt jñāna asinā a chitvā śeṣam karma bandhanam mā a kāma kṛtam śitvā śuddhaḥ tu ātmani tiṣṭhati yathā vanhiḥ mahā dīptaḥ śuṣka māca nirdahet tathā āśu bha aśubham karma jñāna agniḥ dahata īkṣaṇān krīḍan na lipyate jñānī tadvat indriya pannagaiḥ tadvat sarvāṇi pāpāni jīryate jñāninām kṣaṇāt yathā jñānam tathā dhyānam jñānam dhyānam samam smṛtam jñāna dhyāna rataḥ saukhyam muniḥ mokṣam ca vindati sarveṣām eva yajñānām dhyāna yajñaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ mahā dhyāna yajñaḥ paraḥ yajñaḥ sthūlaḥ śuddha śva karmaṇām antaryāga upacāreṇa yaḥ pūjayati śaṃkaram dhyāna yajñena satatam sayāti paramām gatim yama ādi niyamaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ātma ekādaśabhiḥ paraiḥ tapas yajñaḥ tapas yajñaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ daśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ xc japa yajñaḥ tapas yajñāt jñeyaḥ śataguṇa uttaram jñāna dhyānena mucyate prakṣīṇa aśeṣa pāpasya jñāna dhyāne bhavet matiḥ dhanuṣām koṭibhiḥ yogaḥ tad ardhena hutāśanaḥ gaṅgā carṣa aṣṭabhiḥ śvāpaiḥ dharmakṣetram tad ardhāt agnau kriyāvataḥ devaḥ thṛdidevaḥ manīṣiṇām pratimāsu alpa buddhīnām jñāninām sarvatas śivaḥ śivam ātmani paśyanti pratimā suna yoginaḥ yaḥ smaret sarva gaṃśa antam śivaḥ sadā mārgati te śivam divasam divasa ardham vā yatra tiṣṭhati yoginaḥ mahā pāṣāṇa vāhibhyaḥ na tat syāt ratna vāhinām śrama śveti vināśaḥ vā nityam pāṣāṇa vāhinām tad śuddha bhāvena śivam kṣaṇa ardha dhyātvā param mukti karam viśuddham syuḥ na bahiśvarāḥ tathā antar dhyāna tiratāḥ priyāḥ śambhoḥ na karmiṇaḥ yathā antar davinaḥ datāḥ sukhinaḥ na bahis sthitāḥ tathā antar dhyāna niratāḥ sat phala an abahiśvarāḥ yena saṃprāpyate jñānam mahā artham gūḍha gocaram vairyātāca sahāya tvāt suhṛda aiśvayathā gajaḥ vipadyeta jñāna yoga artham udyataḥ mṛdu madhya uttamā ca eva śraddhā puṃsām tridhāma tā yanma trayāt jñāna yogam aśraddhā upi iha vindati bhaktyā śivāt tam āpnoti tad jñānāt paramam padam iti evam jñāna yogasya māhātmyam samudāhṛtam tad abhyāsa ratānām ca munīnām śānta cetasām manaḥ karma yoga rata ātmanām śata janma bhavat dānam tapas niṣṭhāya dīyate tathā alakṣa guṇam dānam pradhānam śiva yoginām ati alpam api yat dānam śiva jñāna artha vādinām tad dānam alpam bahu vā kiṃcid asti vijānataḥ deśa kāla vidhi śraddhā pātra dattam ta dakṣayam pātre deśe ca kāla ca vidhinā aśraddhā yācayat dattam kṛtam hutam phalam bhavet tila ardha mātrakeṇa api parimāṇena dīyate yat dhautam jñāna salilaiḥ śīla bhasma pramārjitam tat pātram sarva pātrāṇām uttamam sārvakāmikam tat pātram paramam smṛtam na ajñānī tārayet ajñam kim śilā tārayet śilām śiva yogī gṛhe yasya bhikṣām gṛhṇāti satkṛtām jñāninā śānta cittāya śivaṃdhyāna ratāya ca ekam muni varam śāntam īśāna arpita mānasam bhojayitvā āsa rud bhaktyā āsa rvān kāmān avāpnuyāt tatas sākṣāt śivena etat su bhuktam aśanam bhavet maheśivāya sarva pāka annaṃnive grāma nauca homayet yoni vedyā tmanā bhuṃkta sa rudraḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ kṛṣi vṛddhi ādi vāṇijya krodha sammārjana ādi bhiḥ puṃsām sūnā doṣaiḥ tu pañcabhiḥ sammārjana añjanam toyam agnikuṇḍa nipeṣaṇam nityam pāpa abhivṛddhaye śiva agni guru pūjābhiḥ pāpaiḥ etaiḥ na lipyate paṣṭikāḥ ṣaṣṭi rātreṇa pacyate bhāli kalama śālayaḥ śāli viśeṣāḥ majjanam sūpa ādi rasa annam śarkarā dīpa ācitam annam khaṇḍābhyāṃkṛtaiḥ ādibhiḥ vaktā śrotā anumantā ca prayoktā dūṣaṇasya ca etaiḥ tu yaḥ su saṃpa kīṃpaṃca etaiḥ nārakāḥ smṛtāḥ ajñāna paṅka nirmagnam ātma trāṇa vivarjitam tat dānam ajñe tathā anyaḥ tam saha pātreṇa naśyati yat vījam ūṣare nyastam sarva niṣphala tām vrajet jñāna agni rahite vipre tathā dānam nirarthakam yathā ṣaṇḍhaḥ vara strīṣu yathā gauḥ gavi niṣphalā brāhmaṇasya tathā janma jñāna hīnasya niṣphalam tathā adātā agrahītā capatati andhetamasya taḥ yat kāruṇyāt sarva bhūtebhyaḥ śraddhayā yat pradīyate dānam tat api vijñeyam sārvakāmikam uttamam bāla vṛddha kaśā āturān etān saṃpūjayet nityam arthī gṛha ati nityaśas arhatva ajñāninaḥ pātram sa spṛhā tvāt nata īrthinaḥ dātuḥ eva upakārāya gṛham adānāt tasya dāridrcam dānāt aiśvaryam āpnuyāt tasmāt dātā avrajet ūrdhvam adhas tiṣṭhet pratigrahī yat idam kaṣṭam arthi tvam prāk adāna phalam hi tat cante dehi iti rūpaṇam janāḥ avastheyam adānasyam ābhūt evaṃbhavān iti iti kalyāṇa māyā antam arthinam kaḥ na pūjayet māyā atyarthī gṛham dātuḥ kaḥ tam na pratipūjayet tad arthinaḥ syuḥ katham pūjya a yācamāna dinedine muttānakam kṛtvā dānam gṛṇhāti yaḥ dijaḥ dānāt ūrdhva gatiḥ tena dātuḥ darśaya tīva saḥ ekena tiṣṭhatā adhastāt anyena upari tiṣṭhatā dāḍha yācakayoḥ bhedaḥ karābhyām eva sūcitaḥ yaḥ prāpte arthini dīne tu tyaktvā apācam pratīkṣate yadi lubdhāḥ sat ādīn asyuḥ apriya vādinaḥ kutradā ānandayā akṣāṃtiḥ bhāvyaṃte sādhubhiḥ tathā yadi nāmana deyam syāt svam saṃprāpta arthine gṛhe kiṃvākyāni apinaṣṭāni priyāṇi anugatāni ca abhyutthāna abhigamanam svāgatam svāsanam priyam cittam vitta anusāreṇa kadā kasya bhaviṣyati svabhāvāt dāna kāmaḥ yaḥ sa svargī na atra saṃśayaḥ dānam priya vinirmuktam naṣṭam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sa kanda api iha dātavyam priyeṇa akṣayam icchatā pratyākhyānam api śreyas priya anunaya peśalam asatkāra pāruṣya malina arutam varam na dattam arthibhyaḥ saṃkruddhena antarātmanā tapaḥ yaḥ śraddhayā arthinā idadyāt pratigṛṇṃti ca arthinaḥ audārya saṃgatam maitrīm anukampām amatsaram mahitān pañca dātuḥ dānam mahā phalam ca ca mahāpuṇyaḥ gokarṇaḥ jñānaparvataḥ ityādi kīrtita ādeśāḥ sura siddhaiḥ niṣevitāḥ sarvam śiva āśramam puṇyam sarva anadyaḥ sa parvatāḥ tat ananta phalam jñeyam śiva kṣetra anubhāvāt dinacchidra aṇi saṃkrāntiḥ yugāṃta aśvayuga ādayaḥ ete kālāḥ samākhyātāḥ puṃsām puṇya vivardhanāḥ bhakti bhāva yutam kāle dānam dattam sadā akṣayam mātā iva jananī jñānasya sukṛtasya ca tad nanta phalam teṣām apigrāsāḥ ī mātrakam pradattam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharma saṃhitāyām saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tad traye pāpa nilayāḥ sthūlāḥ naraka hetavaḥ te samāsena kathyate vāc manas kāya saṃsthitāḥ para strī dravya saṃkalpam ceta sa aniṣṭa cintanam akārya abhiniveśa śva caturdhā karma mānasam abhakṣya bhakṣaṇam hiṃsā mithyākārya niveśanam para svānām upādānam caturdhā ākarmakāyikam mahādevam saṃsāra arṇava tārakam su mahā pātaka upetāḥ te yānti nirayam narāḥ dūṣayanti śivam śātra jñānam sarva artha sādhakam su mahat pātaiḥ kim teṣām niraya arṇava gāminām ye śiva jñāna vaktāram nindaṃti ca tapasvinam arṇavam śiva nindā guroḥ nidā śiva jñānasya dūṣaṇam haranti ye ca saṃmūḍhāḥ śivam jñānasya pustakam mahāntipātakāni āhuḥ ananta phala dāni paṭ na abhinandanti ye dṛṣṭvā śiva pūjām prakalpitām nanamanti acitam dṛṣṭvā pūjitam na stuvaṃti ca yatheṣṭa ceṣṭā niḥśaṅkāḥ saṃtiṣṭhate ramanti ca sthāna saṃskāra pūjām cayena kurvati parvasu vidhivat vā gurūṇām ca karma yoga vyavasthitāḥ ye tyajanti śiva ācāram śiva bhaktāḥ dviṣanti ca tad a saṃpūjya śiva jñānam ye dhīyate likhanti ca ca vikrīṇanti ca lobhena ku jñāna niyamena vā tad asaṃskṛta pradeśeṣu yatheṣṭam sthāpayaṃti ca śiva jñāna kathā akṣe payaḥ kṛtvā anyasya bhāṣate aśuciḥ vā aśuci sthāneyaḥ pravaktiḥ śṛṇoti ca yaḥ śākham śrotum icchati tad na karoti ca śuśrūṣām ājñām bhakti ca bhāvāt ca gurum ārtam aśaktam vā videśa prasthitam tathā vairibhiḥ paribhūtam vāyaḥ saṃtyajati pāpa kṛt tad bhāryā putra mitreṣu yaśva avajñām karoti ca evam su vācakasya api guroḥ dharma anudarśiṇaḥ su mahā pātakāni āhuḥ śiva nindā samā nica mahāpātakinaḥ tu ete tad saṃyogī ca pañcamaḥ krodhāt lobhāt bhayāt deṣāt brāhmaṇasya vadha ituyaḥ brāhmaṇam yaḥ samāhūya uktvā paścāt dadāti na udāsīnam sabhā madhye brahmahāsa prakīrtitaḥ mithyā guṇaiḥ yaḥ ātmānam nayati utkarṣatām balāt dehānām para dopān parijñāya nṛpa karṇe japet tuyaḥ pāpīyāḥ piśunaḥ kṣudraḥ saca vai brahma hā bhavet gavām tṛṣā abhibhūtānām dvijānām guru pūrvakam deva dvija gavām bhūmi pradattām haratetuyaḥ praṇaṣṭām api kāla natamāḥ huḥ brahma ghātakam ca brahmahatyā samam jñeyam pātakam na atra saṃśayaḥ yaḥ kiṃcid vivratam gṛtya niyamam yajanam tathā tyāgī pañcayajñānām surā pāne na tat samam tyāgi kūṭa sākṣī dvije anṛte apriyam śiva bhaktānām abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇam maneniraparādhānām prāṇinām ca upaghātanam iti pāpāni ghorāṇi brahmahatyā samā tu dīne sarva sva haraṇam nara strī gaja vājinām moṃ padhīnām rasasya ca candana aguru karpūraiḥ kastūrī paṭa vāsasām hasta nyāsa apaharaṇam rukma steya samam smṛtam kanyānām varaiḥ yogyānām adānāt sadṛśe vare tyaja strī niṣevaṇam savarṇāya avagamanam guru bhāryā samam smṛtam mahāpātaka tulyāni śṛṇudhvam upapātakam dvija dravya apaharaṇam maryādāyāḥ avyatikramaḥ atyanta viṣaya āsaktiḥ kārpaṇyam śāṭhya matsaram para dāra abhigamanam sādhu kanyāsu dūpaṇam putra mitra kalatrāṇām bhāve svāminaḥ tathā tyāgaḥ ca parityāgaḥ sādhu bandhu tapasvinām gavām kṣatriya vaiśyānām strī śūdrāṇām tathā vadhaḥ mahā āśrama tarūṇām ca puṣpa ārāma vināśanam yaḥ pīḍām āśrama sthānām āca ret alpakām api kupya dhānya paśu steyam apāṭhyānām ca pāṭhanam yajña ārāma taḍāgānām dāra apatyasya vikrayaḥ tīrtha yātrā upavāsānām vrata āyatana karmiṇām strīdhanāni upajīvaṃti strībhiḥ atyanta nirjitāḥ arakṣaṇam ca nārīṇām madyapa strī niṣevaṇam mālāgata apradānam ca dhānya vat hi upasevanam ninditasya dhana ādānam viṣama araṇya yantrāṇām satatam vṛṣa vāhanam uccāṭana abhicārau caḍhatya ādāna bhiṣaj kriyāḥ kāma upabhoga artha yasya ārambhaḥ su karmasu mūlyena adhyāpakaḥ nityam veda jñāna ādikam tyāga anya ācāra niṣevaṇam asat śāstra adhigamanam śuṣka tarka avalambanam deva agni guru sādhūnām nindā gobrahmaṇasya ca pratyakṣam vā aparokṣam vā rājñām maṇḍalinām api duḥśīla anāstikāḥ pāpāḥ sadācāra vādinaḥ strī putra mitra samprāptau āśā āccheda kara āśvaye janasya apriya vaktāraḥ kūrāḥ samaya bhedinaḥ bhettā taḍāga kūpānām saṃkramāṇām rasasya ca eka paṅkti sthitānām capāka bhedam karoti yaḥ iti etaiḥ khīnarāḥ pāpaiḥ upapātakinaḥ smṛtāḥ yuktābhiḥ tathā anyāni śṭaṇutāni bravīmi te ye go brāhmaṇa kanyānām svāmi mitra tapasvinām kāryāṇi para śriyā abhitapyaṃte ye para dravya sūcakāḥ yaḥ sevate dvijaḥ śūdram surān ca āghrāti kāmāt hiṃsā priya a narāḥ paṃkti arthaye pi kurvam ti dāna yajña ādikāṃ kriyām goṣṭha agni jala rathyā su taru chāyā nageṣu ca tyajati ye purī ṣa ayam ārāma āyataneṣu ca madya pāna rata anarāḥ kṛta keli bhujaṃga aśva randhra anveṣaṇa tatparāḥ ṣaṣ iṣṭakā śilā kāṣṭhaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ śaṅkubhiḥ eva ca ye mārgam anuruṃdhati para sīmām haraṃti ye kūṭaśāsana kartāraḥ kūṭa karma kriyā ratāḥ kūṭa yuddha anna vastrāṇi kūṭa saṃvyavahāriṇaḥ dhanuṣa śastra śalyānām kartā ayaḥ kraya vikrayī śvayaḥ mithyā pravadatā uvāca ākarṇayati yaḥ śanais svāmi mitra guru drohī māyāvī capalaḥ śaṭhaḥ bhāryā putra āpta mitrāṇi bāla vṛddha kṛśa āturān bhṛtyān atithi bandhūn a tyaktvā aśnāti bubhukṣitān yaḥ svayam miṣṭam aśnāti viprebhyaḥ na prayacchati vṛthak pākī sa vijñeyaḥ brahma vādiṣu garhitaḥ niyamān svayam ādāya yeti ajanti ajita indriyāḥ krūrāḥ śapante ca muhur muhur ha puṣṇanti satatam ye tyajanti ca pīḍayanti ca bhāreṇa satatam vāhayanti ca saṃyatān na vimucati hayas bhāra ākrānta roga ārtān goṭapān ca kṣudhā āturān tuṣṭi arthaiḥ ājñena pālayanti yatnena go ghnāḥ tena nārakāḥ smṛtāḥ vṛṣāṇām ṭapaṇāni eca pāpiṣṭhāḥ gālayanti ca narāḥ vāhayaṃti ca gām vandhyām mahānārakiṇaḥ narāḥ āśaya a samanuprāptān kṣudh tṛṣbhyām śrama karśitān atithīn śva tathā śreṣṭhān sva śaktyā gṛham āgatān anāthān vikalān dīnān bāla vṛddha kṛśa āturān na anukampanti ye mūḍhāḥ te yānti naka arṇavam gṛheṣu arthāḥ nivartate śmaśānāt api bāndhavāḥ māhiṣikaḥ sāmudraḥ vṛṣalī patiḥ śūdra vat kṣatra vṛtti śva nārakāḥ syuḥ dvija adhamāḥ mahā śilpinaḥ kāravaḥ vaidyāḥ hemakāra nṛpa dhvajāḥ bhṛtakāḥ kūṭa saṃyuktāḥ smṛtāḥ yasya rājñaḥ prajā rāṣṭre pacyate narakeṣu ca ye dvijāḥ pratigṛṇhanti nṛpasya anyāya vartinaḥ mayān tate tu ghoreṣu narakeṣu na saṃśayaḥ pāradārika corāṇām caṇḍānām vidyate tu agham yat tat arakṣakasya api rājñaḥ bhavati nityaśas ghṛta taila anna pāna ādi madhu māṃsa surā āsavam guḍe suśarkarā annāni dadhi mūla phalāni ca tṛṇa kāṣṭha pattra puṣpam auṣadham vāsa bhājanam upānah chattra śakaṭam āsanam ca kamaṇḍalum trapu tāmra ārasīsa niśaṅkha ādyam ca jala udbhavam ca anyat gṛha upakaraṇāni ca mūrṇā kārpāsa kauśeya paṭṭasūtra uddhavāni ca sthūla sūkṣmāṇi vastrāṇi ye lobhāt diharanti ca evamādyāni ca anyāni dravyāṇi vividhāni ca apahṛtya naraḥ yāti narakam na atra saṃśayaḥ śarīra yātanā arthāya pūrva ākāram avāpnuyāt yama lokam trajati ete śarīreṇa yama ājñayā deva tiryañc manuṣyāṇām adharma nirata ātmanām dharmarājaḥ smṛtaḥ śāstā a su ghāraiḥ vividhaiḥ vadhaiḥ niyama ācāra yuktānām pramādāt skhalita ātmanām prāyaścittaiḥ guruḥ śāstā anabuddheḥ iṣyate yamaḥ pāradārika caurāṇām anyāya vyavahāriṇām nṛpatiḥ śāsakaḥ proktaḥ pracchannānām ca dharmarāj tasmāt kṛtasya pāpasya prāyaścittam samācaret yathā na abhuktasya anyathā nāśaḥ kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api pāpa gatiḥ phalam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām pāpabhedādikathanam nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha pāpaiḥ naraḥ āyānti yama lokam caturvidhaiḥ saṃtrāsa jananam ghoram vivaśāḥ sarva dehinaḥ strī put napuṃsakaiḥ jīvaiḥ jātavyam sarva jantuṣu śubha aśubha phalam tatra dehinām saṃvicāryate na kecid prāṇinaḥ saṃti yena yāṃti yam akṣayam tatrayeśuta karmāṇaḥ saumya citta ādaya anvitāḥ te ghoreṇa pathinā āyāṃti dakṣiṇena yama ālayam ṣaṣ aśīti sahasrāṇi yojanānām ti iti asaḥ samīpa stham iva ābhāti narāṇām śubha karmaṇām prāṇinām api dūra stham pathinā araudraṇa gacchatām tīkṣṇa kaṇṭaka yuktena śarkarā nicitena ca tīkṣṇaiḥ pāpāṇaiḥ nicitena ca ke cit paṅkena mahatā a duruttāraiḥ ca pātakaiḥ taṭa prapāta viṣamaiḥ parvataiḥ vakṣa saṃkulaiḥ pratapta aṅgāra yuktena yāti mārgeṇa duḥkhitaḥ kvacid viṣama garta ādyaiḥ kva ca loṣṭhaiḥ su puṣkalaiḥ saṃtapta vālukābhiḥ śva tathā atīkṣṇaiḥ śrva śaṅkubhiḥ aneka śākhā vitataiḥ vyāptam vaṃśa vanaiḥ kvacid kaṣṭena tamasā mārge anālaṃbena kutracid gāṭakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kvacid dāva agninā avataḥ kvacid vālukayā a vyāpta mākaṇṭha antam praveśitaḥ bhūyas kvacid uṣṭa ambunā avyāsam kvacid cakariṣa agninā makṣikābhiḥ śva raudrābhiḥ kvacid sarvaiḥ viṣa ulvaṇaiḥ matta mātaṃga yūthaiḥ śvabala unmattaiḥ pramāthibhiḥ pathinam ullikhadbhiḥ ca śukaraiḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭribhiḥ tīkṣṇa śṛṅga aiśva mahiṣaiḥ uṣṭraiḥ matta aiśva pādapaiḥ ḍākinībhiḥ śva raudrābhiḥ vikarālaiḥ śva rākṣasaiḥ mahā caṇḍena vāyunā mahā pāṣāṇa varṣeṇa hanyamāna anirāśrayāḥ kvacid vidyut prapātena dāryamāṇau ajanti vā mahatā ā bāṇa varṣeṇa hanyamāna aśva sarvatas patadbhiḥ vajra pātaiḥ śva aulkā pātaiḥ ca dāruṇaiḥ pradīna aṅgāra varṣeṇa datyamānāḥ śvasaṃti ca mahatā apāṃsu varṣeṇa pūryamāṇā rudanti ca niśita āyudha varṣeṇa bhidyamānāḥ ca sarvatas mahā kṣāra ambu dhārābhiḥ siṃcamānāḥ trajanti te mahā āśī tena marutā arūkṣeṇa paruṣeṇa vā samantāt vyāpyamānāḥ ca śuṣyaṃte saṃkuñcaṃti ca mahatā anirjana apāśrayeṇa ca tamas rūpeṇa kaṣṭena sarva duḥkha āśrayeṇa ca nīyam tad dehinaḥ pāpa karmiṇaḥ yamadūtaiḥ mahā ghāraiḥ tad ājñā kāribhiḥ balāt mitra bandhuvi varjitam hocantaḥ svāni karmāṇi rudanta muhur pretībhūta avi vastra aśva śuṣka kaṇṭha uṣṭha tālukāḥ bhaya bhītā bhaya bhītā kṣudhā agninā baddha śṛṅkhalayā kecid uttāna pādayoḥ narāḥ kṛṣyaṃte kṛṣyamāṇāḥ ca yama dūtaiḥ bala utkaṭaiḥ urasā adhomukha aśvān ye ghṛṣyamāṇāḥ su duḥkhitāḥ keśa pāśa nibandhena samākṛṣyanti rajjubhiḥ lalāṭa īcām kuśena anyebhiḥ nāḥ kṛṣyanti dehinaḥ uttānāḥ kaṇṭaka pathinā kvacid aṅgāra vartmanā paśu ādvāhuka baddha aśva jaṭhare ca prapīḍitāḥ pūritāḥ śṛṅkha lābhi śva hastayoḥ śva su kīlitāḥ grīvā pāśena ruṣyanti prayati anye su duḥkhitāḥ jihvā aṃkuśa praveśeṇa samākṛṣyaṃti rajjunā nāsā bhedena rajvā casamākṛṣyanti ca apare bhinnāḥ kapolayoḥ ajjvā aruṣyanti anye tathā oṣṭhayoḥ ākhaḥ karṇayoḥ karṇayoḥ ca anye bhinna aśva cibuke pare kāḥ saṃbhinna śiśna vṛpaṇāḥ chinna bhinna aṅga saṃdhayaḥ ita śveta śvadhāvanti kandamānā nirāśrayāḥ bhindipālaiḥ vibhiyante sravantaḥ pūya śoṇitam mad yācamāna aśva salilam annam vā api bubhukṣitāḥ chāyām prārthayamāna aśvaśīta ārtāḥ ca analam punar dāna hīnāḥ prayānti evam prārthayataḥ sukham narāḥ gṛhīta dāna pātheyāḥ sukham yānti yama ālayam evaṃnyāyena kaṣṭena prāptāḥ preta puram yadā prajñāpitāḥ tadā dūtaiḥ niveśyanti yama agratas tad traye śubha karmāṇaḥ tān tu sat mānayet yamaḥ tad svāgata āsana dānena pā dya arthyena priyeṇa vā dhanyāḥ ayūyam mahātmānaḥ ātmanaḥ hita kāriṇaḥ idam vimāna mārutya divya strī bhoga bhūṣitam tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān ante puṇya sya saṃkṣayāt dharma ātmānaḥ narāya ica mitra bhūtam iva ātmanaḥ saumyam sukham prapaśyanti dharmarājānam eva vā bhayānakam haṃsa karāla vadanam bhṛkuṭī kuṭila īkṣaṇam ūrdhva keśam mahā śmaśrum ūrdhva visphurita adharam aṣṭādaśa bhujaṃkūram nīlāñjana caya upamam mahā mahiṣam ārūḍham dīpta agni sama locanam mṛtyuḥ ca eva samīpa sthaḥ kāla anala sama prabhaḥ kālavāñjana saṃkāśaḥ kṛtāṃtaḥ ca bhayānakaḥ mārīca ugra mahāmārī kālarātriḥ ca dāruṇā vividha avyādhayaḥ na arūpa bhaya āvahāḥ śakti śūla aṃkuśa dharāḥ pāśa cakra asi pāṇayaḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ mahā vīrāḥ kūra añjana mahā prabhāḥ sarva āyudha udyata kara ayama dūta abhayānakāḥ yamam paśyaṃti pāpiṣṭhāḥ citraguptam ca bhīṣaṇam jīva a duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ para dravya apahārakāḥ garvitā rūpa vīryeṇa para dāra avamardakāḥ tat kim ātma upaghāta artha bhavadbhiḥ duṣkṛtam kṛtam idānīm kim pratapyadhvam pīḍyamānāḥ sva karmabhiḥ aivam te ṭathivīpālāḥ saṃprāptāḥ tad samīpatas bho bho nṛpa a durācāra a prajā vidhvaṃsa kāriṇaḥ alpa kālasya rājyasya kim tvayā duṣkṛtam kṛtam mohena balāt anyāyāt prajāḥ yaiṃḍitāḥ phalam tasya bhujyadhvam adhunā a nṛpāḥ tat sarvam saṃparityajya yūyam ekākinaḥ sthitāḥ paśyāmi tad valam naṣṭa yena vidhvaṃsitāḥ prajāḥ yamadūtaiḥ gṛtyamāṇāḥ adhunā kīdṛśam bhavet tūṣṇīm tiṣṭhati pārthivāḥ iti dharma samuddiśya nṛpāṇām dharmarājya maḥ tad pāpa paṅka śuddhi artham idam vacanam abravīt bho bho caṇḍa mahācaṇḍa gṛhītvā nṛpatīn balāt niyamena viśodhadhvam krameṇa naraka agniṣu tatas samādāya nṛpam saṃgṛtya pādayoḥ drumāḥ niḥsaṃjñaḥ sa tad ādehī niśceṣṭaḥ saṃprajāyate tatas tatas sa vā ayubhiḥ spṛṣṭaḥ sa taiḥ ujjīvyate punar tatas pāpa viśundhi arthe kṣipanti naraka arṇave aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ evāyāḥ kṣiti adhas tatra koṭayaḥ atighorā amahāghorā aghorarūpā ca pañcamā bhayānakā tad aṣṭamī kālarātri śva navamī ca bhaya utkaṭā daśamī tad adha khaṇḍā mahācaṇḍā tatas upi adhas caṇḍa kolāhala cā caṇḍa caṇḍa caṇḍa caṇḍa tara ca bhīṣṭā bhīmā bhīmapraṇāyakā karālā avikarālā cavajjā viṃśatimā smṛtā trikoṇā pañcakoṇā ca sudīrghā aparivartulā samabhauma aṣṭabhaumā ca dīptā māyā iti ca aṣṭamā iti tena amataḥ proktā aghorā naraka koṭayaḥ tāḥ eva etāḥ prāpa anāṃyātana ātmakāḥ tāsām krameṇa vijñeyāḥ pañca pañca eva nāyakāḥ pratyekam sarva koṭīnām nāmnaḥ tān nibodhata mahāraurava pīḍābhiḥ mahantaḥ pi rudanti ca tamaḥśītam tathā ca uṣṇam pañca ādyāḥ nāyakāḥ smṛtāḥ su ghoraḥ su mahā tīkṣṇaḥ padma saṃjīvanaḥ śivaḥ mahātama vilaḥ paśca suloma śvāpikaṇṭakaḥ tīvra vega karāla śva vikarālaḥ prakampanaḥ suprapīḍanaḥ kumbhīpākaḥ supāka śvakrakaca śvāpi dāruṇaḥ aṅgāra rāśi bhavanam medosṭa prahitaḥ taḥ tīkṣṇatuṇḍa śvaśakuniḥ mahāsaṃvartakaḥ kratuḥ tapta jantuḥ paṅka lepaḥ pratimāsas trapu udbhavaḥ ucchāsaḥ muniḥ ucchrāsaḥ sudīrghaḥ kūṭaśālmaliḥ pradītaḥ su mahā nādaḥ pravāhaḥ supravāhanaḥ tatas megha aṃṭapaḥ śalyaḥ siṃha vyāghra gaja ānanāḥ tad ka rāja mahiṣa avikārava kānanāḥ mīna vakra ākhyāḥ sarpa kūrma ākhya vāyasāḥ mṛdha ulūka jalaukā ākhyāḥ śārdūlaka vikarkaṭāḥ maṇḍūkaḥ pūtivakra śva rajataḥ pūtimṛttikaḥ ma śvabhojanaḥ lālābhakṣa ātmabhakṣāḥ ca sarva bhakṣaḥ su dāruṇaḥ tanaḥ añcarīpaḥ kaṭāha śva kaṣṭā vaitaraṇīnadī su tapta loha śayanam meka pādaḥ prapūraṇaḥ asita āla vanam ghoram asthi bhaṅgam supūraṇam tila atasī suyantra āṇi kūṭa pāśaḥ pramardanaḥ mahācūrṇī sucūrṇī catama loha mayaḥ tathā mūtra viṣṭhā śukapaśca tārakūpa aśru aśītalāḥ musala ulūkhalam yantram śilā śakaṭa lāṅgalam tāla pattra gahanam mahā śakaṭa maṇḍapam hālāhala śva yama anugaḥ deva pādaḥ śvāva carantimaḥ te kramaśas pañca pañcakam koṭīnām ānupūrvyam ṇa pañca pañca eva nāyakāḥ raurava agram avīci antam narakāṇām śatam smṛtam catvāriṃśat śatam proktam mahānaraka maṇḍalam prapacyaṃte śopyaṃte naraka agniṣu tābhiḥ vicitrābhiḥ sva karma prāyāt bhṛśam tatra pāpa kṣayāt pāpa anarāḥ karma anurūpāt su gāḍham hastayoḥ vaddhāḥ tapta śṛṅkhalayā narāḥ kiṃkaraiḥ dolantaḥ ca api vegena visaṃjñāyanti yojanam antarikṣa sthitānām ca lohaiḥ bhāra śatam punar pādayoḥ badhyate teṣām yamadūtaiḥ mahā balaiḥ tena bhāreṇa mahatā su bhṛśam tāḍitāḥ anarāḥ dhyāyaṃti svāni kamaṇi tūṣṇīm dhyāyaṃti niścalāḥ tatas uṃ'kuśaiḥ agni varṇaiḥ loha daṇḍaiḥ vakaṇṭakaiḥ hanyate kiṃkaraiḥ ghoraiḥ samantāt pāpa karmiṇaḥ tatas kṣāreṇa dīptena vanheḥ api viśeṣataḥ samaṃtataḥ pralipyaṃti tīvreṇa ca punar punar hrutena atyanta liptena kṛtta aṅgāḥ jarjarīkṛtāḥ punar vidārī acāṅgāni śirasaḥ prabhṛti kramāt viṣṭhā kūpe tathā kūpe rumīṇām nicaye punar medas sṛj pūya pūrṇāyām vā api ākṣipyanti te punar hakṣyam tena mibhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ lohatuṇḍaiḥ śva vāyasaiḥ te matsya vat ca api pradīpta aṅgāra rāśiṣu su tīkṣṇaiḥ śva narāḥ pāpena karmaṇā tila vat saṃprapīḍyaṃte cakra ākhya jana pīḍakāḥ bhujyaṃte ca ātapa itame loha bhāṇḍeṣu anekadhā taila pūrṇa tap iṣu punar punar bahudhā pāṭyate jivhāye asatya priya vādinaḥ sudaṃśena sutamena prapīḍya urasi pādayoḥ jivhā ardha kośa vistīrṇā hilaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ prapīḍyate nirbhartsa yaṃtiyekūrā mātaram pitaram gurum tatas kṣāreṇa dīptena tākhena ca punar punar itas tatas punar vakram bhṛśam āpūrya hanyate viṣṭhābhiḥ kamibhiḥ ca āpipūryamāṇāḥ kvacid kvacid pariṣvajanti ca ati ugrām pradīptām loha śālmalīm hanyate pṛṣṭha deśe ca punar dīmaiḥ mahā ghanaiḥ dantureṇa ati kuṇṭhena krakacena balīyasā śiraḥ prabhṛti pīḍyante ghoraiḥ karmabhiḥ ātmajaiḥ hāyaṃte ca sva māṃsāni pāyaṃte śoṇitam svakam anna pānam na dattam yaiḥ sarva dāsu ātma poṣaṇaiḥ ikṣu vat saṃprapīḍyante jarjarīkṛtya mudgaraiḥ asita āla vanaiḥ ghoraiḥ chigranta īkhaṇḍa khaṇḍaśas sūci nirbhinna sarva aṅgāḥ tamas śūla praropitāḥ saṃcālyamānāḥ bahuśas kliśyan tena mriyaṃti ca yathā svapna śarīrāṇi sukha duḥkha sahāni ca dehāt utpāṭya māṃsāni bhiyante asthīni mudgaraiḥ punar ākṣipyate tūrṇam yama dūtaiḥ bala utkaṭaiḥ ucchrāsyanti tathā ucchrāsya vālukā vadanenarāḥ raurabera uda māna aśva pīḍyante vividhaiḥ vadhaiḥ mahāraurava pīḍābhiḥ mahantaḥ pi rudanti ca padbhyām āsye gude gaṇḍe ca akṣiṇā ūśva urasi mastake te ghanaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ sutamaiḥ loha śaṅkubhiḥ sutapta vālukāyām ca prayojyaṃte muhur muhur jantu paṅkebhṛśam tama īkṣitāḥ kandanti visvaram tena tena eva rūpeṇa śāsyate pāradārikāḥ gāḍham āliṃgate nārīm jvalatīm loha nirmitām pūrva ākāra aśva puruṣa aprajvalam duśvāriṇīm striyam gāḍham āliṃgaṃti hasaṃti ca kim pradhāvasi vegena na te mokṣaḥ asti sāṃpratam laṃghitaḥ te yathā bhartā pāpam bhuṃkṣva tathā adhunā yathā yathā yathā mṛddagninā prapacyaṃte sva pāpaiḥ eva mānavāḥ kṣipanti ulūkhala lepī enam prapīḍyate śilāsu ca kṣipyate ca andhakūpeṣu daśyate bhbhrameraiḥ bhṛśam tad sarva aṅgāḥ śataśas jarjarīkṛtāḥ su tīkṣṇa kṣāra kūpeṣu kṣipyate tat anantaram mahājvāletu narake pāpāḥ kandaṃti duḥkhitāḥ dhāvanti dhāvanti tad arciṣā pṛṣṭhe ca ānīya jaṅghābhyām vinyastā skaṃdha yojite tayoḥ madhyena vāruṣya bāhu pṛṣṭhena gāḍhāt badhvā parasparam sarvāḥ su bhṛśam pāpa rajjubhiḥ pīḍya baddhāḥ su dṛśyate bhramaraiḥ tīkṣṇaloha jaiḥ māninām krodhinām ca eva taskarāṇām ca dāruṇāḥ piṇḍa baddhāḥ tatas yāmyaiḥ mahā jvālena yātanāḥ rajjubhiḥ veṣṭyamāna aśva praliptāḥ kardamena ca su tīkṣṇa kṣāra toyena karkaśā suśilāsu ca māsphālya prakṣayāt pāpāḥ āghṛṣyaṃte candanam yathā harīra abhyantara gataiḥ prabhūtaiḥ kamibhiḥ narāḥ bhakṣyaṃte tīkṣṇa vadanaiḥ ādeha prakṣayāt bhṛśam bhūya māṃsa sya rāśiṣu tiṣṭhati udvigna hṛda yāḥ parvatābhyām nipīḍitāḥ adhomukha ūrdhva pāda aśva dhṛtāḥ tapyanti vanhinā tekhā daṃti para adhīnāḥ tājyaṃte tusu mudgaraiḥ kāmāya udvartana abhyaṅga snānapānām bhojanam krīḍanam maithunam dyūtam ācaram ti mada uddhatāḥ deva agni iṣu pacyaṃte yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam te śṛṇvanti karṇaḥ prapūryate tatas agni varṇaiḥ ayaḥ kīlaiḥ tatas tāmra ādibhiḥ kṛtaiḥ trapu sīsa āra kūṭābhiḥ kṣāreṇa ca punar punar su tapta tīkṣṇa tailena vajña lepena vā punar bhayāt āpūryate karṇaiḥ naraka iṣu ca yātanāḥ sarva idriyāṇām api evam kramāt pāpena yātanāḥ bhavanti ghorāḥ pratyekam śarīra tad kṛtena ca sparśa lobhena ye mūḍhāḥ spṛ śanti ca para striyam teṣām kara ugni varṇābhiḥ pāṃsubhiḥ pūryate bhṛśam tatas kṣāra ādibhiḥ sarvaiḥ śarīram anulipyate sarveṣu narakeṣu ca pitroḥ netrān ca ye narāḥ para dārān ca paśyanti lubdhāḥ stabdhena cakṣuṣā sūcibhiḥ agni varṇābhiḥ kṣārāyai śva kramāt sarva dehe sarva aśva yātanāḥ śivāya deva agni guru viprāṇām a nivedya prabhuṃjate pāṇinā jighaṃticanara āmūḍhāḥ śirasā ādhārayaṃti ca maṃta śiraḥ teṣām saṃtamaiḥ loha śaṅkubhiḥ mahulaiḥ tatas kṣāra ādibhiḥ bhṛśam ye nidanti mahātmānam vācakam dharma deśakam deva agni guru bhaktān ca dharmaśāstram ca śāśvatam tepām urasi kaṇṭhe ca jivhā āryā dinta saṃdhiṣu tāluni oṣṭhe ca jivhāyām mūrdhani sarva aṅga saṃdhiṣu taptāḥ ca triśi khā loha śaṅkavaḥ māvidhyaṃte ca bahuśas sthāne pu etad iṣu mudgaraiḥ tatas prapūryate samaṃtataḥ trāḥ śarīrasya api sarvatas niḥśeṣam nara ketu evam bhramanti kramaśas punar ye gṛṇhaṃti para dravyam padbhyām vipram spṛśaṃti ca vā upakaraṇa aṃgam ca jñāna ādi likhitam ca yat hasta pāda āghanaiḥ teṣām āpūryate samaṃtataḥ narakeṣu ca sarveṣu vicitrāḥ dehayātanāḥ bhavanti bahuśas kaṣṭāḥ pāṇi pāda samudbhavāḥ śivāyatana paryante deva ārāmeṣu kutracid samutsṛjanti ye pāpāḥ purīṣam mūtra me teṣām śiśnam sa vṛṣaṇam cūrṇyate loha mudgaraiḥ sūcibhiḥ agni varṇābhiḥ tathā ca āpūryate punar tatas kṣāreṇa mahatā atī tailena āpūryate gāḍham gudaṃśinam ca dehinaḥ manaḥ sarva iṃdriyāṇām ca yasmāt duḥkham ca jāyate dhane sati api yedāḥ naṃna prayacchaṃti tṛṣṇayā atithi ca avamanyate kāle prāptam gṛha āśrame teṣām ca vivṛtam vai kaṅkīlaka dvaya tāḍitam cotraiḥ lohatuṇḍaiḥ śva vāyasaiḥ śyāmaḥ ca śabalaḥ ca eva yama mārga anurodhakau yauḥ taḥ tābhyām prayacchāmi tau gṛhṇītam imam valim indra vāruṇa vāyavya āyāmya nairṛta vāyasāḥ śaivaiḥ mantraiḥ balim paścāt dadaṃti yenateyamam paśyanti tridivam yānti tasmāt dadyāt dine dine maṇḍalam catur akham ca kṛtvā gandha adhivāsitam dhanvantare īśānyām prācyām indrāya niḥkṣipet yāmyām yamāya vāruṇyām sudakṣomāya dakṣiṇe viniḥkṣipya trāyām aryamaṇetataḥ dhātuḥ ca eva vidhātuḥ ca dvārapebhyaḥ śva niḥkṣipet vayobhiḥ kṛmi kīṭaiḥ śva gṛhasthaḥ śva upajīvyate svāhākāraḥ svadhākāraḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ stutīyakaḥ svāhākāram tatā devāḥ svadhām ca pitaraḥ tathā hantakāram haṃtakāram manuṣyāḥ ca pibanti satatam stanam yaḥ tu etām mānavaḥ dhenum śraddhayā amara pūrvakām kṣudhā ārtam atithim samyak eka grāma a nivāsinam bhojayet tam śubha annena yathāśakti ātma bhojanāt duṣkṛtam da tvā apuṇyam ādāya gacchati punar jivhā vegena baddhaḥ tra ciram kālam satiṣṭhati tatas tat māṃsam utkṛtya tila mātra pramāṇāt teṣām khāditum dīyate teṣām bhitvā ca eva tu śoṇitam api niḥśeṣa yātanābhiḥ tu pīḍyam kramaśas punar ati bubhukṣayā akaṣṭam tathā ca ati pipāsayā evamādyāḥ mahā ghora āyātanāḥ pāpa karmiṇām dharma gurutaram vā api tathā avasthā aṃtayoḥ yaḥ guru dharma api sa upavāsaḥ yathā gṛhī tāni pāpāni ghorāṇi saṃtīhayaiḥ tatas naraḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca kṛta pāpa anara āyati duḥkhena mahatā anvitāḥ hi śubha aśubham atha u vakṣyetān dharmān mukha dāyakān traye śubha karmāṇaḥ saumya citta ādaya anvitāḥ yaḥ pradadyāt dijendrāṇām upānah kāṣṭha pāduke sa vara aśvena mahatā asukham yāti yama ālayam śivikāyāḥ pradānena tad rathena sukham vrajet hi śayyā āsana pradānena sukham yānti su niścayam hartāraḥ vai janti vṛkṣa ropakāḥ yāṃti puṣpaka yānena puṣpa ārāma kara anarāḥ devāyatana kartāraḥ yatīnām āśramasya ca tad tad tad tad tad ca krīḍayanti gṛha udare deva agni guru viprāṇām mātā pitroḥ ca pūjakāḥ yathāsukham dyotayantaḥ diśaḥ sarva āyānti dīpa pradāyinaḥ pratiśraya pradānena sukham yānti nirāmayāḥ viśrāmyamāṇa aga chanti guru śuśrūṣaka anarāḥ ātta aiṣadha pradātāraḥ mukham yānti gṛhe svake yena datta anna pānāni tṛptā yāṃti hi tad patham pāda śauca pradānena śītalena pathinā vrajet bhyaṅgam cayaḥ kuryāt aśva pṛṣṭhena saḥ vrajet tathā abhyaṅgam dīpam annam pratiśrayam raupya anaḍḍāha dānena naraḥ yānena gacchati sarva kāma samṛddha ātmā bhūmi dānena gacchati iti evamādibhiḥ dānaiḥ sukham yānti yama ālayam svarge tu vividhān bhogān prāpnuvanti sadā narāḥ sarveṣām eva dānānām anna dānam param tat annāt bhavanti bhūtāni tad abhāve mriyaṃti ca rakta māṃsa vasā śukra kramān ātma vardhate mad bhavanti bhūtāni tasmāt anna mayam jagant nāga indraiḥ nārī sraj kandana ādibhiḥ hāram abhikāṃkṣaṃti deva dānava rākṣasāḥ kṣudhā ahi sarva rogāṇām vyādhiḥ śreṣṭhatamaḥ smṛtaḥ tathā anna auṣadha lepena naśyatī hana saṃśayaḥ na asti kṣudhā sama duḥkham na asti rogaḥ kṣudhā samaḥ tathā akṣudhā agninā ataptā mriyate sarva dehinaḥ annadaḥ prāṇadaḥ proktaḥ prāṇada śvā api sarva daḥ yasya anna pāna puṣṭa aṅgaḥ kurute dharmam saṃcayam anna pradātuḥ tasya ardham kartuḥ ca ardhana saṃśayaḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām dehaḥ parama sādhanam annam prajāpatiḥ sākṣāt annam viṣṇuḥ svayam śivaḥ tasmāt anna samam dānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati trayāṇām api lokānām udakam jīvanam smṛtam pavitram amṛtam divyam śuddham sarva rasāyanam kṛtvā api su mahat pāpam yaḥ paścāt anna daḥ bhavet anna pānāt ca go vastra śayyā chattra āsanāni ca preta loke praśastāni dānāni aṣṭa viśeṣataḥ evam dāna viśeṣeṇa dharmarāja pure narāḥ tapasā prāpyate svargaḥ tapasā prāpyate yaśaḥ āyuḥ praharṣaḥ bhogaḥ ca labhyaṃte tapasā mune mārogyam rūpavat tvam tathā eva ca yat ca dūram durārādhyam su dūram duratikramam dhanam prāpnoti tapasā maunena ājñām tathā eva ca ahiṃsayā balam rūpam dīkṣayā janma sat kule phala mūla āśinām rājyam svargaḥ parṇa āśinām bhavet payaḥ bhakṣaḥ divam yāti sthānam ca draviṇa adhikam striyaḥ triṣavaṇam snātvā a vāyum pītvā kratum labhet maunam sādhayate rājyam nāka pṛṣṭham anāśake thaṃḍila itu śayāna agṛhāṇi śayanān iva cīra valkala vāsobhiḥ vāsāṃsi ābharaṇān iva śayyā āsana aniyāna aniyoga ātmani tapodhane rasāṇām pratisaṃhāre saubhāgyam iha viṃdati miṣam pratisaṃhāre prajā asya āyuṣmatī bhavet satya vādī nara śreṣṭhaḥ daivataiḥ saha modate dvija śuśrūṣayā arājyam dvija tvam ca ati puṣkalam tṛpyante kāma bhogāt sāṃtva daḥ sarva bhūtānām sarva duḥkhaiḥ vimucyate deva śuśrūṣayā arājyam divya rūpam niyacchati loke pradīpa dānena cakṣuṣmān bhavati prabhuḥ prekṣaṇīya pradānena smṛtim medhām ca viṃdati gandha mālya anida tva ca kīrtiḥ bhavati puṣkalā keśa śmaśru dhārayatām agryā bhavati saṃtatiḥ upavāsam ca dīkṣām vā api abhiṣekam yathākramam viśiṣyate dāsī dāsa malaṃkāra kṣetrāṇi vividhāni ca tīrtha upavāsa iśva tridivam yān nimānavāḥ suvarṇa śṛṅgaiḥ su virājita anāḥ gavām sahasram ca naraḥ pradātā yāvati romāṇi bhavanti dhenvaḥ tāvat phalam labhate go pradātā putrān ca pautrān ca kulam ca sarva mā saptamam tārayate paratra sa dakṣiṇām kāṃcana cāru śṛṅgīm kāṃsya upadohām draviṇa uttarīyām dhenum tilānām dadataḥ dvijāya lokāvasūnām sulabhā bhavam te tam sva karmabhiḥ mānavam mahā arṇavān nau paratra yaḥ trahma deyām tu dadāti kanyām bhūmi pradānam cakaroti vipre svādhyāya cāritra guṇa anvita āyatasya api lokān pravadanti nityān dhurya pradānena tathā gavāśvaiḥ lokān avāpnoti naraḥ vasūnām svargāya ca api āḍuḥ hiraṇya dānam tatas viśiṣṭam kanaka pradānam chattra pradānena gṛham viśiṣṭam yānam tathā upānaha sampradāne puppa upagān ceva phala upagān śvayas pādapān yacchati vaidvijāya bhakṣya anna pānasya rasasya dānam sarvān avāpnoti rasān prakāmam tratiśraya ācchādana sampradātā prāpnotitān evana saṃśayaḥ utra sraj dāma gandhā ni anulepanāni snānāni mālyāni ca mānavaḥ yaḥ bījaiḥ a śūnyam śaraṇaiḥ upetam yā gṛham yaḥ puruṣa uddijāya puṇya abhirāmam bahu vatra pūrṇa latī adhiṣṭhāna param muni īśaiḥ su gandha citra āstaraṇa upapannam dadyāt naraḥ yaḥ śayanam dvijāya rūpa anvitām putravatīm manojña bhāryām ayatna upagatām labhet saḥ uvāca yāni yāni tu deyāni dānāni paricakṣate tebhyaḥ viśiṣṭam kiṃdānam kim tārayati tat vada yat ca abhilaṣitam dadyāt tṛṣitāya upayācate dattam dātāram anveti tat śṛṇuṣva mahāmate hiraṇya dānam go dānam pṛthivī dānam eva ca etāni vai pavitrāṇi tārayanti ati duṣkṛtīn dānāni etāni sādhubhyaḥ datvā mucyati pātakāt yat yat iṣṭatamam loke yat ca asti dayitam gṛhe yācamānam abhimānāt anāsaktam akiñcanam taḥ yaḥ na arcati yathāśaktyā asa nṛśaṃsaḥ nara adhamaḥ mitram api ced dīnam śaraṇa eṣiṇam āgatam mate dadyāt dati glānāyayā cate hiyātu niyatān sādhūn putra dāraiḥ śva karśitān a yācamānān kā leyaḥ sarva upāyaiḥ nimantrayet dyā snātām vrata snātā adhyātma gati cintakāḥ mūḍha svādhyāya tapasaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ śaṃsita vratāḥ sva dāra niyata adāntāḥ śaktyā dāna parāyaṇāḥ purāṇa smṛti vettāraḥ yajña karmasu anuṣṭhitāḥ ete pūjyatamāḥ nityam ācāryaḥ sa purohitaḥ yat śubha ārya bhartāram yajamānam tathā dvijaḥ sadā eva sāgatiḥ na anyā kṣatriyāṇām manasvinām brāhmaṇeṣu sadā bhaktiḥ dāna ācchādana bhojanaiḥ yat imā iva āhmaṇaiḥ avyāsaiḥ saṃtyajeyuḥ apūjitāḥ mad abhāvāya brahma sūnunā gataḥ aham dharmarājānam draṣṭum sam pūjitaḥ umayā mayā tatra upaviṣṭena dṛṣṭam kiṃcid mahā adbhutam kāñcanena vimānena vaiḍūrya tavedinā maṇi muktā vicitreṇa kiṅkiṇī jāla śobhinā āgatam puruṣam tatra āsanāt devam sattamaḥ sa sambhramam samutthāya dṛṣṭvā adharmaḥ svayam vikṣuḥ gṛhītvā idam tadā vākyam uvāca samīpe mama tiṣṭhasva yāvat ājñā sata ha āgataḥ puruṣaḥ divyaḥ yatra tiṣṭhati dharmarāj svayam dharmeṇa vai brahman vā apūjām kṛtāṃtayoḥ tatra me vismayaḥ jātaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ mayā tatas naraḥ te sakāśam hiyaḥ yaṃ pūrvam iha āgataḥ kim anena kṛtam karma yasi atuṣṭaḥ bhavān bhṛśam tathā eva āsyaka tā pūjā yaḥ tvam ābhyām samam pūjām kuruṣe dharma kāraṇāt brahma viṣṇu śiva ādyaiḥ pūjyase tvam sadā bhṛśam tat śubham iha āyāti itat śṛṇuṣva mahāmate asti tatra abhūt pṛthivīpālaḥ dharāpāla eti śrutaḥ tatra abhūt pṛthivīpālaḥ dharāpāla eti śrutaḥ kasmin kāle purā devī śaśāpa sva gaṇam kudhā rī bhartuḥ yad ma niveśi tā tasmāt dādaśa varṣāṇi jambukaḥ tvam bhaviṣyasi tatra asau aśanam kṛtvā kṣetre trāṇān tatas sṭajat tatra āśvaryam mahat ṛṣṭvā adharāpālaḥ mahīpatiḥ śambhoḥ āyatanam kṛtvā sthāpayāmāsa vaiśivam hubham āyatanam śambhoḥ tasmin agre sabhājanaiḥ mūrṇa itu brāhmaṇa ādīnām pūjayitvā kadambakam itihāsa purāṇa jña vācakam ca viśeṣataḥ pūjayitvā dija śreṣṭham vidyāśreṣṭham mahā munim pustakam ca api saṃpūjya gandha puṣpa ādibhiḥ kramāt tatas tam āha rājā asau uvāca mayā iha āyatanam śambhoḥ kāritam tu śiva agratas cāturvarṇyam idam ca api śrotu kāmam kadambakam tiṣṭhati iha dvijaśreṣṭhaiḥ kuru pustaka vācanam svarṇa niṣka śatam ca atra tatodāsye tathā aparam hanta iva ṛṣe a dvija śreṣṭha śreyas artham aham ātmanaḥ atha āyuṣaḥ kṣayāt ca ayam kāladharmam upeyivāḥ mayā ācātsya vimānam hiśivena preritam divi iti eṣā a karmaṇā uthyuṣṭiḥ puṇya ākhyānaka saṃjñakā tu na jāyate tathā devānām iha sarveṣām purāṇa śravaṇā yathā grāmāṇām nagarāṇām ca dānāt tuṣṭiḥ bhavet na hi yathā asyāt dharma śravaṇāt prītiḥ sarva divaukasām itihāsa purāṇānām śravaṇam muni sattamaiḥ yathā me syāt mahā trītiḥ na śrāddhaiḥ sarvakāmikaiḥ yaḥ ca ayam aparām vipraiḥ ehi āyātaḥ nara uttamaḥ ca ayam dharma śravaṇam uttamam śrutvā bhaktiḥ abhūt asya tataśva śraddhayā anvitaḥ tvā pradakṣiṇa aṃtasya vācakasya mahātmanaḥ aiṣa vipraḥ muni śreṣṭha pradadau svarṇa māṣakam na anya dāna kadā cakre lobha āviṣṭena cetasā pātra dāna phalāt eṣa prāptavan brahmaṇaḥ padam yat anena rutā pūjā vācakasya mahātmanaḥ tena aham pūjitaḥ sya vaii ka viṣṇu śaṃkaraḥ tathā śrāddhe haṃ pūjitaḥ sya vai i daśa varṣāṇi pañca ca kṛtsraśas devatānām ca aindra ādīnām tathā bhavet brahma viṣṇu śiva ādīnām saṃdeṣṭā vācakaḥ umune prīte tasmin devatāḥ syuḥ sarvāḥ prītāḥ na saṃśayaḥ candra āditya agraha ādayaḥ mad sādhanāya pūjyaṃte tatas saṃpūjyatām gatāḥ snānam pūjā japaḥ homaḥ śrutam śaucam ahiṃsa tā dhī bindya asatyam akrodhaḥ dānam kṣāntiḥ dayā damaḥ vāpī kūpa taḍāgānām prāsādānām ca kalpanam kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇam yajñāḥ tīrthāni sva āśramāṇi ca mad sādhanāni sarvāṇi proktāni iha manīṣibhiḥ duḥkham pāpāt vijānīhi tasmāt dharma mayam sukham trividham tam vijānīhi sattva rājasa tāmasam sadā satvam tapaḥ vidyāt muni siddheṣu nityaśas etat dṛṣṭvā āca śrutvā śyāśam iha āgataḥ lokapitāmahaḥ yau dṛṣṭau bhavatātau tu purāṇau puṇyakāriṇaḥ sūryeṇa api yat uktam hi tathyam vā enān yathā bhavet yadā āsīt mama mukham putraiḥ pañcamaṃloka pūjitam tasmāt etāni sarvāṇi niḥ sṛtāni samaṃtataḥ tad itihāsa purāṇāni lokānām hita kāmyayā yathā etāni mama iṣṭāni purāṇāni sadā mune na tathā caturaḥ veda dāna ca aṅgāni mahāmate vāca bheṭatti nityam śraddhā samanvitaḥ maktyā ate yānti paramām gatim tamam dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām mayāḥ sṛṣṭāni suvrataiḥ itihāsa puraṇābhyām vedam samupabṛṃhayet ye ete caturaḥ veda a gūḍha arthāḥ satatam sthitāḥ atas tu etāni sṛṣṭān ibaḥ dhāya eṣām mahā mune sadā bhaktyā sayā ati paramam padam tat tra param brahma adhigacchati na āścarya pātra dānāt hi dāna pātram hi tatparam tīrthānām iva kedāram vratānām ca mahā vratam parvatānām yayau meruḥ pakṣiṇām garuḍaḥ yathā yathā pātrāṇām api sarveṣām vācakaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ pūjitam sakalam tena jagant syāt na atra saṃśayaḥ aho iti dhanya tātasya dharma śravaṇa kāriṇaḥ dānam yat dadata utyartha puṇya tā vācaka āyave iti śrī śivapurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām śravaṇamāhātmyakathanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śastāni ghora dānāni mahā dānāni nityaśas pātrebhyaḥ tu pradeyāni ātmānam tārayaṃti te hiraṇya dānam go dānam pṛthivī dānam eva ca tau pavitrāṇi tārayanti svam eva tam yat sarva pramucyate tulya dānāni śastāni gāvaḥ pṛthvī sarasvatī deyāni yācamānebhyaḥ pānam annam tathā eva ca eṣa buddhiṃmataḥ yajñaḥ śraddhā pūtaḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ yajñebhyaḥ dadataḥ iti anasūyayā mahā ghorāṇi vakṣyāmi trāhmaṇyam upahanyate tyājyāni asmai dvinā āpadam mṛta śayyā ajinam kṛṣṇam pāpāt vikrayam ātmanaḥ cāṇḍālāt patitāt mlecchāt tathā ca ubhayatas mukhā tulāyām rohaṇaṃdānam kurukṣetra pratigrahaḥ tilaiḥ āpūraṇam kṛṣṇaiḥ dānāni eva pṛthak daśa yaḥ tu ekam pratigṛhṇāti brāhmaṇaḥ jñāna durbalaḥ dātā paṅke yathā ākṣipya pādam aśmani tat tathā saṃyāti paramam lokam yāvat ābhūtasam plavam pravakṣyāmi gati ca eṣām pralobha āthṛta cetasām saṃprāpya su mahā dānam yadi icchet gatim ātmanaḥ rutvā ardhena tu kāryāṇi vadānyaḥ kurute sadā evam san vipra mukhyaḥ api gatim śreṣṭhām prayāti hi kanakam ca tilāḥ nāgāḥ kanyā dāsī gṛham rathaḥ mahādānāḥ gṛhītvā tāni sarvāṇi brāhmaṇaḥ jñāna vid sadā tārayet ca eva ātmānam cana saṃśayaḥ suvarṇa prathamam dānam suvarṇa dakṣiṇā aparā daśa pūrvān daśa parān ātmānam ca ekaviṃśakam apipāpa śataṃru tvāt datvā vipreṣu tārayet suvarṇaye prayacchanti narāḥ śuddhena cetasā devatāḥ te prayacchaṃti samaṃtāt aditeḥ śrutam tasmāt suvarṇa da tvāca dattāḥ syuḥ sarva devatāḥ agniḥ hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇa ca hutāśanaḥ ca sarva veda pramāṇa jña a veda śruti nidarśanāt yat a sūtam yat a vācyam ca duṣṭam hi pūta tām vrajet miṣṭam tat sarvadā mune sarvam āpaḥ śuddhi vajanti hi hemnā tasmāt sadā śuddham hāṭakam vanhi sambhavam dadyāt vataṃsam uddiśya sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt svarṇa daḥ sarva daḥ proktaḥ sarvān kāmān labhet divi vimānena arka varṇena bhāsvareṇa virājitaḥ apsaras gaṇa kīrṇena gandharva gati nādinā tasmāt sva śaktyā ādātavyam kāñcanam mānavaiḥ bhuvi suvarṇaye prayacchanti narāḥ śuddhena cetasā uvāca bahu prakārāṇi mayā aśrutāni aho tvayā uktāni ityāni tāni hi dānam tvam atodharāyāḥ khyātam tvayā apūrvataraiḥ narādhipaiḥ dāna ādhipaiḥ sarva bhujaḥ babhūvuḥ tat eva dānam bhagavan stu idānīm sampad karam sarvam athonarāṇām tat te pravakṣyāmi kṛtam hi yena dāna uttamam tat tu adhu na āśṭaṇuṣva atra eva udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam bubhuje sakalān bhogān sana dvīpavatīm mahīm tatra jitvā sahasrākṣam devaiḥ sārdham balāt tatas ha śāsanam kārayāmāsa svakīyam tatra tatra ha su vismayam abhūt tatra dṛṣṭvā rājyam sukham svakam putrāṇām ṣaṣ sahasrāṇi kośam ca akṣayam eva ca ca sphītiḥ jana par̤hānām cana akāla maraṇam tathā bhāryāyāḥ ca eva saubhāgyam rūpam ca apratimam tathā punar syāt iha saṃprāptiḥ pūrva dharmāt aham munīn pṛcchāmi sarva dharma jñān kariṣye sakalam punar evam saṃcintya rājā asau vasiṣṭham idam abravīt tvad prasādāt muni śreṣṭha rājyam avyāhatam bhuvi rūpam ca apratimam lokam bhāryā amesti su śobhanā śarīra ārogyam aiśvarya dāna śaktiḥ anuttamā su saṃtatiḥ su bhṛtya aśvasā anurāgā aśvame prajāḥ harma hāni śvamena astiśaktiḥ mepālanebhuvaḥ sarvam kṛtāt dharmāt evam prāptam mayā akhilam tat śrutvā vacanam tasya vasiṣṭhaḥ prāhanat nṛpam citayitvā aciram kālam śṭaṇu bhūpa anya janmani avantī nagarī nāma pṛthivyā aja ghanesthitā dharmapālaḥ nṛpaḥ tatram sarva dharma anuśāsakaḥ vasataḥ te tu anādṛṣṭiḥ āsīt ca bahu vārṣikī anna kṣayāt tatas tvam tu gatvā ātuvanam āśrayat phala mūla mahā āśinaḥ bhāryayā ayuktaḥ prāgāt aṅgāra kārakaḥ tasmāt tvam bhāryayā a yukta udārūṇi ādāya sa tvaraḥ prāviśat nagarīm saḥ pivikretu tāni sarvathā na jagrāha janaḥ kaśvid dampatiyoḥ aṭamānayoḥ tatas sāyam kṣudhā ārtau tau dhvanim śuśruvatuḥ tadā vaṇij mukhyasya viprāṇām javhata anta gṛha aṅgaṇe tau gatvā tatra kāṣṭhāḥ nijvālayāmāsatuḥ tadā yasya pūrṇimāyām samāgame tadā rāvhanayoḥ mahābhāga tatratau ūṣatuḥ tadā palānām śatame kasya samupoṣya janārdanam arcayitvā vidhānena vaṇij saḥ pi kṛta ādaraḥ sa abdhi dvīpavatīm rājñ bhaktyā paramayā āyutaḥ sā adṛṣṭāt vīyamānā vai vām kliśyamānayoḥ tam dṛṣṭvā aduḥkha saṃta mauna kṛtam puṇyam āvayoḥ yena īdṛśau bhaviṣyāvaḥ dharantau manasā tu iti prāpta adharma phalāt rājyam tasmāt tvam dehi sāṃpratam tasmāt tvam dehi rāja indra pṛthivīm sarva kāma dām dīyamānān tra paśyaṃti pṛthvīm rukmasya bhaktyāḥ sarva pāpa vinirmuktāḥ teyāṃti paramām gatim mana sāyedhara pradāḥ sa abdhi dvīpavatīm dṛṣṭvā teṣām vākyam tathā tathā cakravartī mahā vīryaḥ pṛthu rāja adhipaḥ bhavat bubhuje pārthivam kṣetram sa deva asura rakṣasām piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ tad dattam ca upajīvanti tathā anye bhūbhṛtaḥ pica sarva ratna samāyuktam sapta dvīpavatīm mahīm śaśāsa dharmeṇa punar na adharmaḥ dṛśyate kutas tena ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna ūna pṛthivīpurā tasya etat abhimānam ca vīrya ca pṛthivīpateḥ rūpam dṛṣṭvā śubhā patnī tasya abhūt ca ati vismayā tatas sā ācita yāmāsa sammṛjya vismitā asatī katham syāt saṃpad eṣām e kim punar anya janmani evam sau hudhā acintya pṛthum ca eva samānudat tatas papraccha sarva jñān brāhmaṇān ādi bhūmipaḥ yadi sa anugrahā abuddhiḥ bhavatām muni sattamāḥ yathā vane su prasāditāḥ ūcuḥ yaḥ tam manasi saṃdehaḥ yaśva sāṃśayikaḥ bhuvi gadiṣyāmaḥ yathānyāyam tam pṛccha adya mahīpate tuṣṭaḥ brāhmaṇa aśnīyāt śiyāt dām dharma saṃśayam iti ukte prāhatān viprān ādirājā pṛthuḥ tadā kathayaṃtu yathāvṛttam kim mayā a su kṛtam kṛtam viprāḥ kiṃca anayā asu cāru aṅgāyāḥ mama patnyā rutam punar yena āvayoḥ iyam sphītiḥ su saṃbhūtā a su durlabhā catvāraḥ aśva apratihata āgatayoḥ mama apṛcchataḥ kośasyām balam ca apratimam mastiśarīra ārogyam uttamam sā ham icchāmi tam jñātum yathā ca iyam aniṃditā tyā bhāryā iyam atiśobhanā bhavat karma yasya aśeṣam idam phalam iti pṛṣṭāḥ narendreṇa samastāḥ te tapodhanāḥ marīcim prerayāmāsuḥ kathyatām iti bhūpateḥ yogam āsthāya su ciram yathāvat ṛṣi sattamaḥ jñātavan ādirājasya sarva pūrva viceṣṭitam tatas bhūpam cintita arthaḥ yata vrataḥ uvāca śṛṇu bhūpāla yasya idam sakalam karmaṇaḥ phalam babhūva tvam purā śūdraḥ para hiṃsā parāyaṇaḥ purā iyam bhavataḥ bhāryā pati trata parāyaṇā tvad citta anugata anityam tava śuśrūṣaṇa īratā niḥsvaḥ bhūtvā a parikṣīṇaḥ pareṣām bhṛtya tām gataḥ tyajyamānā api tvām aniṃditā sādhya āviṣṇoḥ āyatanetvayā nītā hema mayī pṛthvī dhaninaḥ vṛṣalasya tu ayodhyāyām mahā rājakasya bhaktyā anayā saha paricaryā kṛta adātuḥ manasā apuṇya kāṃkṣiṇaḥ sammārjana ādikam sarva kṛtam te bhaktyāḥ nṛpaiḥ niḥśeṣam upaśātim tad pāpam śuśrūṣaṇāt anu sarva kāma pradam karma rukma dhenvāḥ kṛtam tvayā tena idam akhilam rājyam aśe sā jagatī tava evam narendra śūdra tvāt tasya karma parāyaṇaḥ kim punar yaḥ naraḥ bhaktyā pṛthvīm haimīm prayacchati śatam pūrva aparam ca api kulānām tārayet nṛpa yāvat candra śva sūryaḥ ca yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī idam yaḥ śṛṇuyāt nityam paṭhet ca eva iha bhaktyāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca evam śrutvā sa rājā atu pṛthuḥ vainyaḥ pratāpavān yādṛśīm kārayāmāsa yad pramāṇām yad udbhavām pañcaviśe hema mayyāḥ sa abdhi dvīpa yujaḥ bhuvaḥ svar upadāna māhātmyam yathāvat upavarṇyate ha ha mānava āloke śaktyā dātuḥ labhaṃti te lakṣaṇa suvarṇena sahasreṇa śatena tu suvarṇena tu kārayet eka hastām dvi hastām vā tri hastām vā apikām atas hema abhāve su tāmrasya kṛtvā kṣipet ratna abhāvāt aṇuṣu eva haimam teṣu vinikṣipet meroḥ bhāge vipula śva uttare tatas tad bhāvāt hiraṇyam tu mauktika ādi tatas param tat kadamba jambuka aśvattha śrīpaṇa pallavam kramāt nāga vayāḥ tathābhāvāt samyak pattrāṇi vinyaset tena āpūrya tatas dvīpaḥ śālmali śvāparaḥ mune tena eva āpūrayet tatas tu dugdhena śāka dvīpam atas param tasmāt tam madhunā āpūrya tad ante puṣkaram sthitam saṃkṣepāt kathitam vyāsaiḥ pṛthivī ādānam uttamam mā asya a varṣa ayutena api vaktum śakya uti vistaraḥ hasta mātram khanet kuṇḍam homam tatra eva kārayet hutvā hutvā pṛthivi iti punar hutvā pūjayet tatra keśavam sarva āśrayaḥ tvam hi pumān aśeṣaḥ sṛṣṭā tvayā iyam pṛthivī dhṛtā a punar dātā tvam asyāḥ pratisaṃgrahītā tubhyam mayā ahema mayā niveditā gṛhṇīṣva kāma abhimanaṃdadasva brāhmaṇān vācayitvā agre prīyatām dharaṇīdharaḥ evam datvā dvijebhyaḥ tān ṭaṇuka āle ca yat phalam śatam tārayitvā divam yāti yāvat indrāḥ caturdaśa prāpnoti bhū tale kramāt mokṣam avāpnoti dānāt asyāḥ prabhāvāt iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām paṃcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca saṃśayaḥ sarva tattva jñaḥ udānāt tvam būhi pṛcchataḥ yat tat uktam purātena tat dānam būti aśeṣatas yena dānena sadyaḥ na a pāpāt bhavati akilbiṣī yat sādhayet nirja deham kṛtvā pāpāni aśeṣa tas jīvam hi daihikāḥ deha sampīḍayā tābhyām naraḥ pāpāya mucyate tasmāt pṛccha ṛṣi śreṣṭha sāṃpratam kathayāmi te asmin kali yuge martyāḥ sat ācāra vivarjitāḥ bahu pāpa ratā mūḍhāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahā mune raurava ādi pu ghorāṇām yātanāḥ kila śuśruma kāntāram gahanam tatra tad artham brūhima idvijaiḥ yathā an apaśyet kāntāram su duṣpāram su durgamam uvāca śṛṇu rājñ mahā gutyam mahāpātaka nāśanam taram yena paśyanti tathā vakṣyāmi suvrataiḥ tasya asite pakṣe caturdaśyām samāhitaḥ tila prastha mayam kṛtvā nāgam sarva guṇa anvitam dhenum vatsam suvarṇa tusu dīpaiḥ sarvatas citam tilaka upetam karṇa cāmara bhūṣitam kāṃsya ghaṇṭā yuga yutam kṣauma kakṣa vibhūṣitam mauktika āpūrṇa kumbhamantu sindūra avata mastakam muktā mālā virājitam pādukā upānaham chattram bhājana āsana darpaṇam kuryāt tasya agre iṣṭa dalam padmam saṃlikhet kuṅkuma ārutaiḥ āpūrya āpūrya acyutam īśānam arcayet kaṇikā pade dhātāram viśva kartāram pūrva pattre tu vāsavam pitṛṇām pataye dharmāya ānaṃda dāyine namaḥ pitṛṇām pataye dharmāya ānaṃda dāyine namaḥ upāṃpataye tubhyam bhava bhīta ti hāriṇe namaḥ te pṛṣat aśvāya vāyave jagat āyuṣe namaḥ te paśu nāthāya śivāya īśāyate namaḥ tāra pataye dhātre trahmarudrāya viṣṇave viśvarūpāya devāya śarmadāya namaḥ namaḥ atra evam kalpa vidhānena tatra kāntāra devatāḥ devadevam tatas abhyarcya viṣṇum viśvapatim punar imam uccārayet mantram kṛta añjali puṭaḥ sudhīḥ kān tāram adhvanaḥ mārgam ibhena anena keśavaḥ cintāmaṇiḥ tathā dantī sadā bhavatu mama vibho dadyāt rāhmaṇāya sva śaktitas sa ratnam sa hiraṇyam ca sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam tatas tatas naktam samaśnīyāt dīpam dadyāt tathā gaje bhārthive rāja śārdūlaiḥ kārttikyām vā pradāpayet hatvā pāpāni aśeṣāṇi sa bandhuḥ samutsṛj janaḥ divisaṃkrīḍatevyāsa yāvat indrāḥ caturdaśa kapilānām śate datte yat phalam jyeṣṭhaiḥ puṣkare tad samaṃsyāt muni sattamaiḥ tad phalam na atra saṃśayaḥ saṃnihatyām nara śreṣṭha rāḥ hu graste divākare harā dāna anna tat puṇyam kāntāreṇa yat aśnute tat puṇyam bhūyas śataguṇena ca puṇyam tat sakalam labhyam mune kāntārahastinā gaja aśva ratha dhenūnām yat phalam hi nigadyate tat phalam sakalam vidyāt kāntāreṇa mahā mune tila ājya jala dhenūnām yat pūrva uktam phalam labhet tad mūrti tanmayīm da tvā puṇyam śataguṇam labhet evam jñātvā muni śreṣṭha śreṣṭha kāntāra kāraṇam dadyāt anena mantreṇa saṃpūjya gaja puṃgavam namaḥ kāntāra rūpāya parameśāya śambhave namaḥ ūṣṭa diś ibha īśāya namaḥ rūpāya viplave tilaka antāra danti dānena daitya hā prīyatām puṃḍarīkākṣaḥ prabhuḥ kāntāra tārakaḥ evam uccārya tat dadyāt brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine paṭhatām śṛṇva tām ca api yaḥ tu bhāvayate sadā iti śrī śivapu0 dharmasaṃhitāyām ṣaḍūiṃśaḥ a dhyāyaḥ uvāca pūrva uktaṃ te dinā ekena pūjitaḥ sa maheśvaraḥ gurūṇām na bhavet kuca vacanam mukha niḥsṛtam mā mām īśvarāt vadatām varaiḥ nāsatyam etat uktam mama ṭaṇu vākyam mahā mune tathā vṛthak śramaḥ hi bahubhiḥ kleśaiḥ na eva aśnute phalam lokānām hita kāmena kṛtam yena iha tat vada uvāca āsīt pūrva yuge rājā jambūddīpe su dhārmikaḥ śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca ādhipatyam cakāra saḥ mad rāja astra vidām śreṣṭhaḥ veda śāstra athaṃpāragaḥ dharmiṣṭhaḥ satya vāc śūra udātā abhoktā atithi priyaḥ dadāti anudinam vyāsa teṣām artha striyā ādikam evam rājyam śurutvā dīrgha kālam mahīpatiḥ hatānīkaḥ tatas nāmnā sahasrānīkam eva ca sutam jajñe tatas kālāt sitīśaḥ saumṭāt tu saḥ pulakam āgatam rājyam ca kresau nṛpa sattamaḥ nyāyatas dharmatas ca eva rājye śāsti vasuṃdharām kāntyā candramasaḥ ca eva pratāpa āditya saṃnibhaḥ truṣu evam sadāpātiḥ pṛthivīṃnyāyatopisaḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dadāti īśaḥ yathā tasya pitā anasaḥ atha dīrghena kālena brāhmaṇāḥ teyata vratāḥ tān āgatān sa saṃprekṣya pūjām cakre yathāvidhi pūjitāḥ te su saṃdṛṣṭāḥ procuḥ nṛpati sattamam ūcuḥ śṛṇu rājñ pravakṣyāmi ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ mahā pitrā te pūjitā nityam dāna ācchādana bhojanaiḥ ye kecid brāhmaṇāḥ saṃti yathākāmam yathāsukham tad saṃvardhitāḥ svaka idhā agni sama buddhiḥ ayam nṛpaḥ mām pratam tava rājye tu saṃprekṣya ca gatāḥ dvijāḥ vasā meotra parikhinnān nṛpate sa kuṭumbinaḥ itas kim kurma evam hiyāsyāmaḥ kutra pīḍitāḥ daridreṇa eva no buddhiḥ yathā śṭaṇu nṛpa uttamaiḥ paratra nyāyāt viprāḥ kiṃcid vakṣyāmi kāraṇam dānāt svargam avāpnoti iha āyātaḥ sukhībhavet samuttasthuḥ samājñāpya rāja ānam dīna mānasāḥ samavāyīkṛtāḥ ste tu tathā anyonyam abhāṣata rājā apañcatvam āpannaḥ kva asau tiṣṭhati dhārmikaḥ vayam katham na jānīmaḥ saṃśayam paramam gatāḥ rājñām dharmavatām ca api prajāḥ pālayatām saḥ tām tasmāt subhikṣam kṣemam eva hi pādityāt jāḥ yate dṛṣṭiḥ vaṣṭeḥ an na samudbhavaḥ annāt saṃjāyate sarvam jagat tṛptiḥ tu sarvadā evam saṃcitya bhagavān ājagāma tatas uraviḥ tāyateṣām saṃdeṣṭum dvijaḥ bhūtvā atutān travīt kiṃviṣaṇṇāḥ dvijāḥ yūyam iha īpsataḥ sva karma tat bahūni śubhatī rthāni phala dāni iha sarvatas śrūḥ yatena phalam dātum sva karma phala hātinaḥ pañcayajña phalam nityam catur āśrama vāsinām tu naimittā labhet puṇyam śata uttaram sahasra guṇitam kāmyāt tathā āpnoti pumān sadā yaḥ tam mṛtam samākhyāsye t tad purāt āgata ud nṛpam tatas tena veṣayāmāsuḥ harṣāt tvā caturdiśam tayāvidham na paśyantaḥ pattaneṣu pureṣu ca gatvā apaśyan tapasi atam bhārgavam dvijasattamam ūrdhva bāhum nirālambam pādena ekena saṃsthitam tam dṛṣṭa a praṇipatya āśu parivārya dvijottamam ca japyam tyaktvā su saṃtarpya devān pitṛ gaṇān tathā upaviṣṭān samadrākṣīt kṛtāñjaliḥ sa pūrvavat pūjayāmāsata ān sarvān pādya ādyaiḥ vidhi pūrvakam paryapṛccha yathānyāyam phala mūlaiḥ su tarpitān tatas te sarvam ācakhyuḥ rājñaḥ durvṛttam ātmanaḥ tathā a dṛṣṭasya viprasya yat vākyam tat niśamyasaḥ manasā ciṃtayāmāsa kim kṛtam sukṛtam bhavet tyajet ahaṃtapaḥ kim vā api athavā ārti vināśayet prāṇinām bhaya bhītānām abhayam yat pradīyate aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi yojanāḥ naḥ pramāṇāt yama mārgasya ca adhvānam ācakrāma divākaraḥ na jalam na ca tatra annam vṛkṣa chāyā sukham nahi hītam śītam vāta andhakāram tu duḥsaha deva dānavaiḥ tu madhya etāsām yayau raviḥ paśyan sa brāhmaṇaḥ tām tu yātanām pāpa karmiṇām ekaikam nirayam tadvat śrūyate kandatām ravaḥ tadā alakuṭa pāṇinā bho bho dvija kkaya yayya yāmada tvām amama dakṣiṇām tayā adattā te purām atyam kasmin kāle tu tām smara iti uktaḥ satutām smṛtvā pratyuvāca dvijam prati uktam mayā purāṇa ekam tubhyam tena asmi yācitaḥ gṛham gatvā pradāsyāmi tirobhava mama agratas tam āha asau dvija ste sti su kṛtam yat ḷ tam tvayā tvā asau nyāyāt saṃpradāpayan tu gauḥ tasya rakṣitā an atu yācitaḥ ṣaṣ vāc antena dharmasya gṛhītam tasya vaibalāt nistejāḥ aśvā bhavat tasmāt gatum ca agrena śaktavan tatas divākaraḥ taṃtu saṃgṛtya āśu kareṇa vai tam dṛṣṭvā pacyamānam tu kumbha madhya gatam nṛpam kiṃcid mātra samāśvasya śatānīkam uvāca bho bho rājñ pradattāni mahādānāni ṣoḍaśa brāhmaṇebhyaḥ tvayā apūrva ratnam vastrāṇi ca eva hi grāmān va vividhān ca eva nagarāṇi purāṇi ca kasya idam karmaṇaḥ pāpam yat tvam saṃdatya se sadā tat śrutvā prāha tat rājā aśṛṇu vipra yathātatham uvāca mayā dānāni dattāni brāhmaṇebhyaḥ yatas tatas tu bahūni pragṛtya api parebhyaḥ ajñānacakṣuṣā prajā pīḍana saṃtāpāt samudbhūtaḥ hutāśanaḥ tena datyāmi aham viprāḥ preta saṃsthā divāniśam pāpāt su duḥsahāt etat śrutvā vacaḥ rājñaḥ sa vipra śva ātma kāraṇāt mānuṣāṇām hita arthāya paryapṛcchat divākaram uvāca sādhūnām darśanam puṇya tīrtha bhūta ahi sādhavaḥ tena phalate tīrtha sadyas sādhu samāgamaḥ na ca eva akṛta puṇyānām deve bhaktiḥ su jāyate ca yadā a pāpa kṣayaḥ matiḥ tasmāt eva param devam manye ham tvām na saṃśayaḥ mānavaḥ saṃsāre patitaḥ lokaḥ kṣetra dāra gṛha ādiṣu kim na prāpnoti saṃmūḍhaḥ svarga mokṣa sukhāni ca śṛṇu vipra yathātathyam lokānām hita kāmyayā pṛṣṭaḥ tehaṃkṛtaḥ te yaḥ dharmaḥ saṃvardhayiṣyati tatas śuddhā sujivhāyāḥ tasmāt āpnoti asaṃśayaḥ devatānām priyam tatra svargāt āryāḥ ānti sarvadā bhuktim ādāya saṃvi hṛtya punar punar saṃtuṣṭāḥ bāla rūpam sa mā āsthāya sukanyā rūpibhiḥ gaṇaiḥ śivāya ca anya devebhyaḥ prekṣaṇam ca mahā utsavam teṣām dhāma tuyānti ete ye bhavanti ati pāpinaḥ tasmāt caturdaśīm ṛuṣṇām śuklām vā samupoṣya ca adyāt dhenum dvijātibhyaḥ śivāya parikalpitām evam hatvā ca pāpāni yāti svargam na saṃśayaḥ etat śrutvā āsa sūryeṇa saha amātya dvijottamān tatas sa rājā atu su saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ śrutvā vacaḥ tasya dvijottamasya saraḥ sa dṛṣṭvā eva nikhanyamānam pṛṣṭvā tu mūlyena cakāra karma dine dine yāvat abhūt suvarṇa tathā ca go mūlyam aśeṣa dānam tatas pradṛṣṭaḥ prayayau sva deśam su rakṣitam mantri varaiḥ tathā nṛpaiḥ dvijopadi ṭaṃma cakāra rājā vratam yathāvat ca tat eva dānam prārutya yānam su vimānam agryam saṃkrīḍamānaḥ sahasā apsarobhiḥ kurute su samyak aikānhikam vyāsa śiva prasādāt labhet divam pūrva pitāmahaiḥ saha nihatya pāpāni purā kṛtāni caturdaśī yaḥ samupoṣya yatnāt daram tu saṃpūjya saṃpūjya dhenum dhenum pradyāt dijasattama āyatasya abhāvāt su ghṛtasya pātram sa vyañjanam vastra yutam saha annam da tvā phalam yat labhate sudhenāḥ nihatya pāpāni purā kṛtāni divam prayāti iha na saṃśayaḥ tra ciram tyuṣitvā āsatuḥ rudra loka rājā ā bhavet atra su dharma śīlaḥ ekām prakuryāt su śubhām vai saṃte caturdaśīm satya yutaḥ samam hi tuṣṭiḥ yathā asyāt iha śaṃkarasya mantreṇa valāt śopi mantra ātmakāḥ sarva aimehi devāḥ su yakṣa rakṣaḥ pitaraḥ manuṣyāḥ sa nakta rātri bhojana sahitā mantrāṇi ca uktāni purā ava te smin taiḥ arcanīyaḥ bhagavant pinākī bhū sukṛcchra hi catur dināni caturdaśī vyāsa a poṣaṇīyā ekādaśyām eka bhaktam sakṛt pānīya me vaca a yācitam tu dvādaśyām sa naktā ca trayodaśī caturdaśī nirāhārā kartavyā acamahāvrate tu godānam phalam ka tvā tat anute cit tvam ātmanaḥ ātmanaḥ mahā śivaḥ saṃprīyatām evam iti uktvā phalam aśnute mad asya samagrasya dravya abhāvāt śṛṇuṣva tat palaiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ pātram śulvasya tu tad ardhakam ghṛtena hiraṇyam tukārayet astreṇa veṣṭayitvā tu tad abhāvāt sa sūtrakam dadyāt tat dijamukhyāya śivaḥ saṃprīyatām miti sthāṇum īśam jagannātham śūlapāṇi maheśvaram praṇataḥ asmi bhūtanātham same pāpam vyapohatu mālinam praṇataḥ asmi jagannātham saṃ mama pāpam vyapohatu candra ardha dhāriṇam devam sarva ābharaṇa bhūpitam triśūla pāṇinaṃtrya kṣatripatha aṃka su dhāriṇam mama pāpam vyapohatu evam pūjya śivam mantraiḥ tatas dānam prakalpayet te tu jāyate bhokriṇaḥ dhanam evam yaḥ kurute samyak caturmāsyāḥ caturdaśīm dvayam yathā śatānīkaḥ yāti asau śāṃkaram padam yaḥ kulānām śatam uddhṛtya nippāpī surapū jitaḥ yat niśāyām tathā prātar yat madhya anha aparāhṇayoḥ saṃdhyāyām ca kṛtam pāpam karmaṇā a manasā a girā iti śrī śiva saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ aṣṭāviṃśe mahā puṇyam śiva nāma sahasrakam tat sarvam nāśam āyāti toya stham lavaṇam yathā evam vā kurute yaḥ tu cāturmāsī vidhānāt evam yaḥ pūjayet bhaktyā caturdaśyām tu śaṃkaram mahasam kīrtayet nāmnām śṭaṇuyāt vā api bhaktyāḥ niyama stthaḥ śuciḥ bhūtvā ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tathayasva samāsena lokānām hita kāmyayā mahā nāmnām sahasram tu iha amutra phala pradam mune śṭaṇu pravakṣyāmi sarva agha ogha vināśanam prakhyātum na api śaktaḥ aham prasādāt ca eva tasya hi prāpya anujñām tatas stotram dhyānam āgāt tat aiśvaram yadā tena abhyanujñātaḥ nevā tadā abhavam yoninaḥ nāmnām kiṃcid samuddeśam vadaye ca avyakta yoneḥ śṛṇu nāma sahasram tu yat uktam padmayoninā daśa nāma sahasrāṇām sahasram tu pitāmahaḥ gireḥ sāram yathā hem tathā etat sāram uddhṛtam śāntikam pauṣṭikam ca eva rakṣaḥ ghnam pāvanam mahat idam bhaktāya dātavyam śraddadhāna āstikāya ca an āśraddadhāna rūpāya nāstikāya jita ātmane yaḥ ca abhyasūyate devaṃbhūta ātmānam pinākinam tad kṛṣṇa narakam yāti saha pūrvaiḥ pitāmahaiḥ tat idam jñātvā anta kāle pi sa gacchet paramām gatim pavitram maṃgalam puṇyam kalyāṇam idam utamam nigadiṣye iti aham vyāsa stavānām uttamam stavam tat tat tat purā kṛtvā sarva loka pitāmahaḥ sarva stavānām divyānām rāja tve samakalpayat tadā prabhṛti ca eva ayam īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ tadā prabhṛti ca eva ayam pareṣām api yaḥ paraḥ hāṃtānām apiyā śāṃtiḥ yutīnām apiyā dyutiḥ tathā yoginām api yaḥ yogī kāraṇānām ca kāraṇam yatas lokāḥ saṃbhavaṃti na bhavanti yatas punar mahā īśaḥ yameśśṛṇu yat śrutvā tvam muni śreṣṭha sarvān kāmān avāpsyasi sthiraḥ sthāṇuḥ prabhuḥ bhānuḥ pravaraḥ vara daḥ varaḥ maṭī vama śikhī khagī sarva aṅgaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ haraḥ ca hariṇa akṣa śva sarva bhūta haraḥ prabhuḥ mavṛtti śva nivṛtti śva niyataḥ śāśvata uddhruvaḥ maśānacārī bhagavant khecara ukhacara udbhavaḥ abhivaṃdyaḥ mahā karmā tapasvībhūtabhāvanaḥ mahī rūpaḥ mahā kāyaḥ sarva rūpaḥ mahā aśanaḥ viśvarūpaḥ virūpaśva viśvabhuj vāmanaḥ manuḥ lokapāla antardhita ātma aprasādā uha ya gardabhī pavitra śva mahant ca eva niyamaḥ niyama āśrayaḥ anādiḥ ādiḥ avyayaḥ saumya rūpaḥ virūpa kṣaḥ somaḥ nakṣatra sādhakaḥ candraḥ sūryaḥ śaniḥ ketuḥ grahaḥ graha patiḥ varaḥ adriḥ adri ālayaḥ kartā amṭaga bāṇa arpaṇa unaghaḥ mahā tapāḥ adīrghatapāḥ adīna udīna sādhakaḥ saṃvatsara karaḥ mantraḥ pramāṇam paramam tapaḥ mahātapāḥ suvarṇaretāḥ sarvajñaḥ subījaḥ vṛṣavāhanaḥ daśabāhuḥ tu animiṣaḥ nīlakaṇṭha aumāpatiḥ viśvarūpaḥ svayam śreṣṭhaḥ baliḥ vairocanoḥ iha ca kamaṇḍalu dharas dhanvī bāṇa hastaḥ pratāpavān aśaniḥ śataghnī khagī paṭṭiśī cāyudhī mahān uṣṇīṣī ca suvakraḥ ca atyugraḥ vinataḥ tathā kṛṣṇaḥ eva ca haṭagāla rūpaḥ sarva arthaḥ muṇḍaḥ kuṇḍī kamaṇḍaluḥ ajaḥ ca mṛgarūpa śvagandhama ālīka parddhapi ha ūrdhvaretāḥ ūrdhvaliṅgaḥ ūrdhvaśāyī nabhastalaḥ tri jaṭī cīra vāsāḥ ca rudraḥ senāpatiḥ vibhuḥ gaja hā daitya hā lokaḥ lokadhātā guṇākaraḥ siṃha śārdūla rūpaḥ ca ārdra śvarma adhara adharaḥ sarvāḥ vāsaḥ catuṣpathaḥ niśācaraḥ preta cārī bhūtacārī maheśvaraḥ tṛpmaḥ nartakaḥ savilāsakaḥ poṣaḥ mahā tapāḥ prāṃśuḥ nityaḥ giri caraḥ nabhaḥ amarṣaṇaḥ umarṣaṇa ātmā ayajñahā kāma nāśakaḥ tathā dakṣa yajña apahārīca supathaḥ madhyamaḥ tathā kṣṇa daśanaḥ ca eva mahākāyaḥ mahā ānanaḥ viṣvaksenaḥ hariḥ yajñaḥ saṃyuga āpīḍa vāhanaḥ tīkṣṇa bāhu śva hari akṣaḥ mahāyaḥ karma kāla vid viṣṇu prasāditaḥ yajñaḥ samudraḥ vaḍavāmukhaḥ lambana ulambita uṣṭha śva bahu māyā payonidhiḥ mahā aṅga śva mahā daṃṣṭraḥ mahā jivhaḥ mahā makhaḥ mahānakhaḥ mahāromā mahākeśaḥ mahājaṭaḥ vṛkṣakāraḥ yakṣaketuḥ taralaḥ vāyuvāhanaḥ maṇḍalī vāyudhām ācade vadānava darpa hā atharva śīrṣaḥ sāma asya ūripu hasta umita īkṣaṇaḥ tathā prakāśaḥ jaṅgamaḥ tathā amogha artha prasāda śva abhigamyaḥ sudarśanaḥ upahāraḥ priyaḥ
