punar kṣatram sa bhārgavaḥ punar śata sahasrāṇi hatvā rājñām mahā yaśāḥ cakāra bhārgavaḥ sarvām mahīm śoṇita kardamām tatas da tvā dvijebhyaḥ tām mahīm sarvām sa bhārgavaḥ punar te kṣatriyā vyāsa trāhmaṇebhyaḥ prajajñire te ca vṛddha amahā vīryāḥ pṛthivīpatayaḥ bhavan brāhmaṇebhyaḥ samādāya balinaḥ pṛthivīm tatas arakṣan śva sutān kāścid stāna kṣatriya yoṣitaḥ tris sapta kṛtvas pṛthivīm dakṣiṇām adadāt prabhuḥ taye tapasā aniyamena ca sa pṛṣṭaḥ tasya ca ācakhyau tulāpuruṣam uttamam sudānam sarva dānānām uttamam pāpa nāśanam bhūtvā artha artha mune śreṣṭha bhārgaveṇa mahātmanā tulā saṃrohaṇam kārya yadi icchet śreyaḥ ātmanaḥ mama kṛtvā apāpāni aśeṣāṇi tulādānam karoti yaḥ pāpa kṛtam yat divase niśāyām dvis saṃdhyayoḥ madhyadine niśā antayoḥ bālena vṛddhena mayā ahi yuvnā a vijānatā ajñāna pareṇa pāpam tat sarvam eva āśu kṛtam nihantu tulā pumān mama haratu smarāriḥ om namaḥ śivāya brahmāṃḍa dānam ukta etat ekatriṃśa ādi pañcabhiḥ brahmāṇḍa rūpam adhyāyaiḥ kīrtyate sa udbhava kṣayam dadāti evam tu yaḥ vyāsa tulāpuruṣam uttamam hatvā pāpam divam tiṣṭhet yāvat indrāḥ caturdaśa iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām tulāpuruṣavarṇanam nāma triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca dānānām tat mama ākhyāhi mānuṣāṇām hita arthāt mānavaḥ ekasmāt ekāt api sarveṣām dānānām tat śṛṇuṣva mama dānānām uttamam dānam brahmāṇḍam khalu mānavaiḥ dātavyam mukti kāmaiḥ tu saṃsāra uttāraṇāya vai sarveṣu eva manonugaiḥ sa bahubhiḥ brahmāṇḍadaḥ krīḍate paścāt yāti param su durlabha padam devaiḥ mune mādhavaḥ uvāca bhagavant brūhi brahmāṇḍam yat pramāṇam yad ātmakam yad ādhāram yathā jātam yena me pratyayaḥ bhavet muneḥ ṭaṇu pravakṣyāmi yat utsedham tu vistaram brahmāṇḍa tu su saṃkṣepāt śṛṇu pāpāt pramucyate yat tat kāraṇam avyaktam śivam padmanāmayam tasmāt saṃjāyate vyoma puṣkarāt vāyu sambhavaḥ tasmāt saṃjāyate brahmā dvīdhā bhūtāt vikālatas tasya ādhāraḥ sitaḥ nāgaḥ sa ca viṣṇuḥ prakīrtitaḥ mā ākhyāya guṇān vaktum na śaktāḥ deva dānavāḥ siddhaiḥ devarṣi gaṇa pūjitaḥ phaṇāmaṇi sahasreṇa svastika amala bhūṣaṇaḥ mada āghūrṇita netrosausa agniḥ śvetā eva acalaḥ sadā eva eka kuṇḍalaḥ sāyaṃgaṃgā pravāhena śveta hāra upaśobhitaḥ da udriktaḥ kailāsa adriḥ iva unnataḥ lāṅgala āsakta hasta agraḥ viśva musalam uttamam upāsyate svayam kanyayā avāruṇyena mūrtayā saṃkarṣaṇa ātmakaḥ rudraḥ viṣa anala śikhā jvalaḥ pātāla mūla sthaḥ sa śeṣaḥ kṣiti maṇḍalam mad sarṣapa vat bhūtam śeṣa uśeṣaiḥ sura arcitaḥ tasya vīryam prabhāvaḥ ca śakyam vā tridaśaiḥ api na hi varṇayitum jñātum sva rūpam rūpam eva ca mālā iva phaṇāmaṇi śilā aruṇā yasya epā sakalā pṛthvī kaḥ tat vīrya vadiṣyati yadā avijṛmbhata enam tomada āghūrṇita locanaḥ tadā acala tibhūḥ eṣā asa adri toya abdhi kānanā guṇānām gacchanti siddha āmuni su kiṃnarāḥ gandharva uraga deva aśvatena anantaḥ yam avyayaḥ muhur śvāsa anila apāḥ tad lohitam haricandanam tasya nāga vadhū hastaiḥ diśām yāti su vāsatām yat sakalam ca eva gaga jyotīṃṣita tvāt yama arāḥ dhya purāṇa ṛṣiḥ nimitta paṭhitam phalam bibharti mālām lokānām śirasā vivṛtā mahī tena iyam nāga vīryeṇa sa deva asura mānuṣā agryam ca eṣām sarveṣām ratna bhūmayaḥ toya prāsāda abhūmayaḥ hema sambhavāḥ teṣu dānava daiteyānām gānām jātayaḥ tathā mahābhāgāḥ rākṣasāḥ daitya sambhavāḥ prāha svargasadām madhye pātālāni iti nāradaḥ nānā ābharaṇa bhūṣā sumaṇayaḥ yatra su prabhāḥ māhlāda kāriṇaḥ śubhrāḥ hate śobhate pānāni bhujyaṃte muditaiḥ bha śam śam tatra vanya ani kamala ākarāḥ nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ramyāḥ manojñāni ambarāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni ati śuśu vāṇi gandha āḍhyam ca anulepanam tapasā asamavāpta anidānavaiḥ siddha mānavaiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām brahmāṃḍakathanaṃnāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ teṣām ūrdhva upariṣṭāt vainaraiḥ kāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva me mama muni śreṣṭha pacyante yatra pāpinaḥ kṛmibhojanaḥ sipattravanam tathā apūya vaha apāyaḥ bahivalaḥ vyadhaḥ sirāḥ saṃdaṃśaḥ kālasūtraḥ catama śva avīci rodhanaḥ śālmalī pacyante te iṣu puruṣāḥ pāpa karma ratāḥ tu ye kūṭa sākṣī antu yaḥ vakti vi bhrūṇa hā apara sva hartā gorodhas viśva ghātakaḥ taiḥ guroḥ vā dhāt vikraya rudh vāla vadhakī keśa vikrayī avamantā agurūṇām yaḥ paśu āddha uktā anara adhamaḥ agamya gāmīya śva api yāti tata khalam dvija maryādā dūṣa kaḥ tathā deva dvija pitṛ ddeṣṭā rana dūṣayitā cayaḥ ha lālā bhakṣe tayā ti ajñaḥ yaḥ śastra kūṭa kṛt naraḥ a yājya yājakaḥ ca eva tathā eva abhakṣya bhakṣakaḥ mitra hā madhu hāya ati krūrām vaitaraṇīm nadīm teḥ uṣṇa iyat iyat antya śauca aśva kuhaka ājīvinaḥ caye ma vratasya vratasya lopaiḥ koya śva sva āśramāt vicyuta āśvaye sam daṃśeyātanā madhye patanti bhṛśa dāruṇe divāsvapneṣu skandaṃti yena rātrahmacāriṇaḥ divāsvapneṣu skandaṃti yena rātrahmacāriṇaḥ ete ca anye ca narakāḥ śataśas tha sahasraśas hi iṣu duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ pacyate yātanām gatāḥ tathā eva pāpāni etāni tathā anyāni saha sraśas bhujyaṃte yāni puruṣaiḥ nara kāntara gocaraiḥ varṇa āśrama viruddham ca karma kurvaṃti ye narāḥ karmaṇā manasā vācāni adhas śirobhiḥ dṛśyam tena arakāḥ divi daivataiḥ devān adhomukhān sarvān na ca paśyanti nārakāḥ thāvarāḥ yona aśva pakṣiṇaḥ paśavaḥ umṭagāḥ dhārmikāḥ tridaśāḥ tadvat mokṣiṇaḥ śva yathākramam yāvantaḥ jaṃtavaḥ svarge tāvantaḥ naraiḥ kaukasaḥ pāpa rudyāti narakam prāyaścitta parāṅmukhaḥ pāpānām anurūpāṇi prāyaścittāni yathā prāyaścittāni kāleya manuḥ svāyambhuvaḥ bravīt yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇām tāni karmāṇi aghāni vai prāyaścittam aśeṣāṇām hara anusmaraṇam param prāyaścittam tu tasya ekam yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate param maheśvaram avāpnoti madhyān hāḥ ādiṣu saṃsmaran prātar niśi ca saṃdhyāyām sadyas pāpa kṣayam naraḥ muktim prayāti svarga āptiḥ samasta kleśa saṃkṣayaḥ tasya antarā ayas vipra indra japa homa arcana ādiṣu śivam aharniśam tasmāt saṃkṣīṇa aśeṣa pātake tat eva prītaye bhūtvā punar duḥkhāya jāyate tasmāt duḥkha ātmakam kiṃcid sukha ātmakam manasaḥ pariṇāmaḥ yaḥ sukha duḥkha upalakṣaṇam jñānam eva param brahma jñānam tatvāya kalpate jñāna ātmakam idam vi śñjñānāt na vidyate paraṃ evam etat mayā ākhyātam sarva naraka maṇḍalam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ hṛṇu tvam vada tomama mali śva kuśaḥ śva puṣkaraḥ ha tu samamaḥ sarve samudraiḥ samabhiḥ ṭatāḥ jambūdvīpaḥ samastānām eteṣām madhyamaḥ sthitaḥ pra viṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt yojanaiḥ tasya ca ucchrayaḥ caturaśīti sāhasraiḥ dvātriṃśat mūrdhani vistṛtaḥ mūleḥ ṣoḍaśa sāhasraḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ himavant hemakūṭa śva niṣadha śvā sya dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaḥ ca śṛṅgī ca auttarevarṣaparvatāḥ daśasāhastrika atyete ratnavantaḥ uruṇaprabhāḥ bhāratam prathamam varṣam tatas kimpuruṣam smṛtam ilāvatam ṛṣi śreṣṭha catvāraḥ ca atra parvatāḥ bhāra citā meroḥ yojana ayutam ucchritāḥ pūrveṇa mandaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ vipulaḥ paścime bhāge supārśva śrū uttare sthitaḥ kadambaḥ jambu vṛkṣa śvapippala uvaṭaḥ eva ca ekādaśa śata āyāmāḥ pādapā giri ketavaḥ mahā dvīpasya yojaṃvūḥ nāma hetuḥ mahā mune mahāgaja pramāṇāni jamboḥ tasya phalāni ca patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvatas raseṇa teṣām vi khyātā tatra jambūnadī iti vai tad pāna svastha manasām janānām tatra jāyate tad pāna svastha manasām janānām tatra jāyate tīremṭat tatra saṃprāpya sukha vāyu viśoṣitā jāmbūnada ākhyam bhavati suvarṇa siddha bhūṣaṇam bhadrāśvaḥ pūrvatas meroḥ ketumālam ca paścime varṣet detu muni śreṣṭha tayoḥ madhya elā vṛtam manaṃcaitraratham pūrve dakṣiṇe gandhamādanam viśvājam paścime tadvat uttarenandanam smṛtam aruṇodam mahābhadram śītodam mānasam smṛtam sarāṃsi etāni ca tu āri deva bhogyāni sarvaśas sītāñjanaḥ kumudaśva kuraraḥ mālyavant tathā meroḥ pūrvatas kesara acalāḥ tathā niṣadha ādayaḥ dakṣiṇatas tasya kesara parvatāḥ bhikhivāsā sa vaiḍūryaḥ kapilaḥ gandhamādanaḥ jārudhi pramukhāḥ tadvat paścimekesara acalāḥ mahīdharaḥ tathā uttare kesara acalāḥ caturdaśa sahasrāṇi brahmanaḥ prathitam divi indra ādi lokapālānām diśāsu vidiśāsu ca tasya samantataḥ ca aṣṭau khyātāḥ puryaḥ samantataḥ samantāt brahmanaḥ puryāḥ tvā indu maṇḍalam viṣṇu pāda viniṣkrāntā gaṅgā patati vaidivaḥ sītā ca alakanandā ca caturdhā pratipadyate mahā pūrveṇa śailāt tu nandā ca eva tu dakṣiṇe girīn atītya sa kalān catur diś su mahā ambudhim sā āyayau prayatā bhūtvā gaṅgā tripathagāminī gandhamādanau teṣām madhya gataḥ meruḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ bharatāḥ ketumāla aśva bhadrāśvāḥ kuravaḥ tathā maryādā āloka bātyataḥ ca kūṭaḥ ca āyāme dakṣiṇa uttare dakṣiṇa uttaram āyātau kaṇikā antar vyavasthitau maṭharāyāḥ sthita ameroḥ yeṣām ddau dvau vyavasthitau kesarāḥ kesarāḥ parvatāḥ eva īśīta āḍhyāḥ su manoramāḥ mahā śailānām antare droṇyaḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitāḥ su ramyāṇi su ramyāṇi tathā teṣu kānana anipurāṇi ca sarveṣām ca eva devānām yakṣa gandharva rakṣasām prīḍanti deva daiteyāḥ śaila droṇīṣu aharniśam dharmiṇām ālaya atyeta bhaumāḥ svargāḥ prakīrtitāḥ na eteṣu pāpa kartāraḥ yānti paśyanti kutracid yāni kimpuruṣāyāṇi varṣāṇi aṣṭau mahā mune svasthāḥ prajā nirātaṅkāḥ sarva duḥkha vivarjitāḥ daśa dvādaśa varṣāṇām sahasrāṇi sthira āyuṣaḥ kṛta tretā ādikāḥ ca eva bhaumāni ambhāṃsi sarvatas kalpanā saptasu etad iṣu nadī aśva su payāḥ svarṇavālu kāḥ śataśas saṃti kṣudra aśvatāṃsu krīḍā subhājanāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām bahmāṃḍa kathanam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ mahat bhāratam himādreḥ ca eva dakṣiṇam uttaram tu samudrasya bhāratī yatra saṃsṛtiḥ nāgaddīpaḥ tathā asaumyaḥ gāndharvaḥ tu athavā aruṇaḥ ayam tu navamaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃvṛtaḥ yojanānām sahasram tu dvīpaḥ yaḥ dakṣiṇa uttaraḥ pūrve kirātāḥ yasyasyuḥ paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ andhrā dakṣiṇatas vyāsa turuṣkāḥ tu api ca uttare brāhmaṇāḥ sa triyā vaiśyā madhyeśūdrāḥ ca bhāgaśas mahendraḥ malayaḥ sadyas śuktimātṛ kṣaparva taḥ samudra kulaparvatāḥ kulaparvatāḥ vedasmṛtī mukhā nadyaḥ pāriyātra udbhavā mune narmadā surasā ādya āśva saṃtya nyāśva sahasraśas sarva pāpa harāḥ śubhāḥ vindhyāḥ dvi nirgatāḥ puṇyāḥ snānāt pāpa bhaya apahāḥ satyapāda udbhavā nadyaḥ kṛṣṇaveṇī ādikāḥ tathā udbhavāḥ triyāmā ṛṣikulyā ādyā mahendra prabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ bhavāḥ nāḥ nā janapadāḥ teṣuvai santomaṇḍaleṣuvai ti se ruta ādīni na ca anyeṣu ddīpeṣu prabhavanti hi dānāni ca atra dīyate ca atra yajvanaḥ yatas hi karma bhūḥ eṣā jambūddīpe mahā mune tatra api bhāratam śreṣṭham atas nyābhogabhūmayaḥ atra janma sahasrāṇām mānuṣyam puṇya saṃcayam gāyanti devāḥ kila gītakāni bhavanti bhūyas puruṣāḥ sura tvāt avāpya mānuṣya mayam kadācid vihṛtya śaṃbhau parama ātma bhūte prāpsyati dhanyāḥ khalu te manuṣyāḥ avayam kṛtāḥ karmaṇi saṃniviṣṭāḥ jānīma taiḥ tad viśivam sukhāyate bhārate ca indriya vipra dhanyāḥ lakṣa yojana vistāram samasta parimaṇḍalam hi mama bhagavant ākhyātam kṣāra udadhi su saṃvṛtam saṃveṣṭya kṣāram udadhim śata sāhasra saṃmitam somakaḥ sumanāḥ śailā vaiśyājaḥ ca eva saptamaḥ vasanti deva gandharvāḥ varṣeṣu eteṣu nityaśas na ādhayaḥ vyādhayaḥ vā api janānām tat tra kutracid daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ anutamā śikhā caiva pāpaghnī tridivā rūpā sana eva anyatra nimnagāḥ haiḥ tāḥ pibaṃti su saṃdṛṣṭāḥ nadīḥ janapadāḥ tu te tatra asti yuga avasthā yathā sthāneṣu saptasu mu ni sattama prāvṛkṣa pramāṇaḥ tu tad madhye su mahā taruḥ ijyate tatra bhagavant śaṃkaraḥ loka śaṃkaraḥ saṃkṣepeṇa tathā bhūyas śālmali tvam niśāmaya sama varṣāṇi tatra eva teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu malena tu vṛkṣeṇa tena śālmali saṃjñitaḥ dviguṇena samudreṇa satatam saṃvṛtaḥ sthitaḥ varṣa āśi vyañjikān agre tāsām nāmāni me śṛṇu hiraṇyāca candrāśukrā vimocanā nivṛttiḥ saptamī tāsām puṇya toyāḥ su śānti dāḥ sana etāni tu varṣāṇi catur varṇa yutāni tu aiṣa dvīpaḥ samudreṇa surodena samāvṛtaḥ dviguṇenakuśa dvīpaḥ samantāt vā ati atas sthitaḥ vasaṃti tatra daiteyām anujaiḥ saha dānavāḥ tathā eva deva gandharvāḥ yakṣāḥ kimpuruṣa ādayaḥ tathā maṇidrumaḥ mahāśailaḥ samamaḥ mandara acalaḥ tu nāmāni śṛṇu tatvāt dhūta pāpa aśivā caiva pavitra asaṃmitiḥ tathā vidyā rambhā mahīcānyā sarva pāpa harāḥ tu imāḥ anyāḥ sahasraśas santi śubha apaḥ hema vālukāḥ kuśa dvī pekuśaḥ tam krauñcadvīpaḥ mahābhāgaiḥ śrūyatām ca romahān dviguṇena samudreṇa dadhimaṇḍa uda kāṭāt varṣa acalāḥ mahābuddhe teṣām nāmāni imā śṛṇu tṛtīyaḥ vā andhakārakaḥ manāk ca eva dundubhiḥ haiḥ kāvarṣa śaileṣu teṣu vai sarva sauvarṇa ramya iṣu sahadeva gaṇaiḥ prajāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdra aśva anukrama uditāḥ santi tatra mahā nadyaḥ sapta anyāḥ tu sahasraśas gaurī kumudvatī ca eva saṃdhyā rātriḥ manojavā bhyāti śvapuṇḍarīka ācayāḥ pibanti payaḥ śubham dadhimaṇḍa udaka śvāpi śāka dvīpana saṃsṛtaḥ dviguṇena adrayaḥ sama teṣām nāmāni imā śṛṇu śyāmaḥ yaḥ tam giriḥ ca eva kesarī mahā vṛkṣaḥ siddha gandharva sevitaḥ tatra pu ṇyā janapadāḥ cāturvarṇya samanvitāḥ nadī aśvātra mahā puṇyāḥ sarva pāpa bhaya apahāḥ yā mahīdharāḥ tathā asaṃtiśataśas tha sahasraśas dharma hāniḥ nateṣu asti svargāt āgatya mānavāḥ parasparam sadā kṣīrodena āvṛtaḥ saḥ api dviguṇena samaṃtataḥ kṣīrābdhiḥ sarvatas vyāptaḥ puṣkara ākhyena saṃvṛtaḥ dviguṇena mahāvarṣaḥ tatra khyātaḥ atha mānasaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi pañca ūrdhva samucchritaḥ tāvatā eva tulakṣāṇi sarvatas valaya ākṛtiḥ tena eva valaya ākāra ddaya varṣa sama ākṛtiḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ nirāmaya avīta śoka arāga dveṣa vivarjitāḥ satya anṛtena tasyāḥ tām sadā eva vasatiḥ sadā tulya veṣāḥ tu manujāḥ hem varṇa eka rūpiṇaḥ puṣkare dhātakīkhaṇḍe mahāvītaiḥ mahāmune tasmin nivasate brahmā apūjyamānaḥ sura asuraiḥ svādu udakena ambudhinā puṣkaram pariveṣṭitam samudraiḥ tu sapta sapta āvṛtāḥ dvīpaḥ ca eva paraiḥ tā teṣām samudra iṣu samā ivai deva atireka aṃśu apakṣayoḥ śukla kṛṣṇayoḥ apām vṛdviḥ kṣayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ śataśas tat daśa uttaram samudrāṇām muni śreṣṭha sarveṣām kathitam tam vai bhojanam puṣkaradvīpe prajāḥ sarvāḥ sadā eva hi tad dviguṇa a hiraṇmaya bhūmiḥ sarva jantu vivarjitā lokālokaḥ tatas śailaḥ sahasrāḥ tad ca tāvat hi yojana ayuta vistṛtaḥ tamas cāṇḍa kaṭāhena sā iyam urvī mahā mune tārā samaddīpā mahīdharā ja ādhāra bhūtā sarveṣām sarva bhūta guṇa adhikā sā iyam dhātrī ca kāleya sarveṣām jagantām ilā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām bhuvanakośavarṇanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tāvat pramāṇa a pṛthivī bhūḥ lokaḥ satuc īyate yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśa eva parisaṃkhyayā paricakṣate raveḥ ūrdhva śaśi ita sthaula kṣayaḥ jana saṃkhyayā grahānām maṇḍalam kṛttram śaśinā upari saṃsthitam saptarṣi maṇḍalam tasmāt lakṣam ekam tu saṃsthitam mahasrāṇām śatāt ūrdhva vyavasthitaḥ dhruvāt ūrdhvam ahar lokaḥ saba ete brahmanaḥ smṛtāḥ sanakaśva sanaṃdaśva tṛtīyaśva sanātanaḥ tathā nirūpya evam mahī gola sūrya ādi sthiti varṇanam śiva mantra śvaparamaḥ pañcatriṃśe abhidhāsyate satya dharma ratāḥ ca eva jñāninaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ mānavāḥ bhuvar loke tu viśvedevāḥ tathā rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ nāgāḥ sura ādayaḥ nava graha gaṇāḥ statra ṛṣayaḥ vīta kalmaṣāḥ pātālāni ca samā eva brahmāṇḍasya ca vistaraḥ ca sarvatas vai samāvṛtam payasā adaśaguṇena sarvatas tat samāvṛtam dvinā vāyunā ca eva nabhasā tamasā tathā bhūtādinā api mahatā daśa uttareṇa veṣṭitam mahantam ca samāgatya pradhānapuruṣaḥ sthitaḥ tasya natasya astisaṃkhya api paramātmanaḥ tena anantaḥ eti khyātaḥ pramāṇam na api vaiyataḥ hetu bhūtaḥ samastasya prakṛtiḥ sā aparā mune aṇḍānām tu sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca īdṛśāṇi prabhūtāni tasmāt avyakta janmanaḥ dārūṇi agniḥ yayā tailam vilaṣu payasi ghṛtam ādi bījāt prabhavanti tatas tebhyaḥ putrāḥ tathā anyeṣām bījāni anya anivaiyataḥ mahat ādayaḥ viśeṣataḥ tat bhavanti sura ādayaḥ bījāt ṛkṣa prarohe ṇa ya thāna apacayaḥ taroḥ maṇeḥ sūrya yadvat dahniḥ prajāyate tadvat saṃjāyate sṛṣṭiḥ śivaḥ tatra na kāmayet śiva śakti samāyoge deva ādyāḥ prabhavanti hi brahma a viṣṇu śva rudra śva sa śivaḥ parigīyate kartā akriyāṇām parigīyate ūcuḥ paḍakṣaram tvayā proktam purā sarva artha sādhakam hi śivasya paramam mantram bhukti mukti karam śivam mayam tu śrotum icchāmaḥ mantrān parama sādhanān yaiḥ purā munayaḥ siddhāḥ śivāt amara tām gatāḥ sūta māṇḍavya ādayaḥ sarva etān sarvāḥ tvam vai dasvanaḥ tam śambhoḥ yat uktam hi purā kila mad bhairaveṇa viśākhasya tat śṛṇudhvam atandritāḥ praṇavam prathamam gṛtya paśvāt devam samuddharet mastaka bindu saṃyuktam pañcamam parigṛtya ca mantraḥ sarva artha sādhakaḥ paraḥ mokṣaḥ paraḥ śuddhaḥ paraḥ dharmaḥ paraḥ vikṣuḥ surā paḥ svarṇa hārīca bhrūṇa hā agurutalpa gaḥ mātṛ hā strī guru ghna śva anyāni uktāni saṃghaśas smaraṇāt mantrarājasya bhasmasāt yati nityaśas sahasraśas koṭi mantra arjitam puṇyam labhate sādhaka uttamaḥ tri saṃdhyam yojapet mantram śatam ekam prayatnāt sampuṭena avarohena na mṛtyoḥ vaśa gaḥ bhavet maṃghayoḥ gulphayoḥ pādayoḥ ca eva sṛṣṭi nyāsa krameṇa tu ādhibhiḥ sādhvasaiḥ anyaiḥ jvara kuṣṭha bhaya ādibhiḥ tat kuryāt divārātram ca sādhakaḥ tri kālam bhāryayā ayuktaḥ yantra ārūḍhaḥ tu sādha kaḥ kumbha mudrām parām badhvā sukha āsana sthitaḥ pumān hetu mantram mṛtyuṃjayam param varṣamā ṇaṃ su dhārābhiḥ sahasra dala saṃyutam evam hi dhyāyataḥ tasya divyam rūpam prajāyate aṇima ādi guṇa avāptiḥ mānasīgati rūpavān sarvajñaḥ uvāca samāsāt vaḥ samākhyātam yat uktam śambhunā āpu rā devyā aśrva kārttikeyena nandinā uktam ṛṣeḥ tu yat namaḥ śivāya ṣaṭtriśe śiva samprīti kārakaḥ yogaḥ uttamaḥ agastya pramukha vipra amunayaḥ vīta kalmaṣāḥ babhūvuḥ mantrarājena jarā maraṇa varjitāḥ babhūvuḥ mantrarājena jarā maraṇa varjitāḥ etat uktam kumāreṇa vyāsasya āmi ta tejasaḥ mayā tubhyam samākhyātam mantram smṛtyu vināśanam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām mṛtyuṃjayoddharaṇam nāma paṃcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca māravyātam punar vakṣyāmi atas param hṛdayam mantrarājasya dhyānam japyam sadā arcanam saṃnihitāni yasya eva vijñānam saḥ ham na asti atra saṃśayaḥ śubhe sidhyanti sarva karmāṇi aṇima ādi guṇāḥ api uvāca śrutam dhyānam mayā deva mantram saṃyataiḥ yogibhiḥ prāpyam na kadācid durātmabhiḥ kāma krodha ādibhiḥ avyākulam jagant dvaṃdva duḥkha śata āviṣṭam indriya arthaiḥ su saṃyutam jagatī īdṛgvidhe deva saṃsāre duḥkha saṃjñite hi tārtha sarva matau nām mokṣa upāyam vadasva me iti uktaḥ tām uvāca idam śṭaṇuṣva ārye yathātatham evam jñātvā caran loke mucyate bhava bandhanāt dvau imau bandha mokṣāṇām na mama iti mama iti ca tri yogaḥ samāsāt kathitaḥ mayā hādevaḥ uvāca jetum rāga ādayaḥ śakyān na tu janma antaraiḥ api uvāca bhagavan tam upāyam mām evaktum arhasi aśeṣatas anāyāsena yene mad nista ranti bhava arṇavam mānuṣāḥ tāḥ śrotum icchāmi tatvāt tasyāḥ tat vacanam śrutvā kṛpā yuktaḥ maheśvaraḥ martyānām hita kāmāya prāha idam pārvatīm tatas uvāca yadi evam mukti kāmā asi mānavānām hitā ayam vai tat śṛṇuṣva kriyā yogam kleśānām hāni kārakam yaḥ tu vāyārtha saṃyogaḥ kriyā yogaḥ saḥ ucyate evam evam mama kriyā yogam su saṃgatam tum śaktaḥ na eva kathaṃcana yaiḥ śūdra aiśvakarma nirataiḥ kriyā yoga āśritam manaḥ kārya liṅga arcane nityam mad anuṣṭhāna tatparaiḥ mad liṅga arcana śaktānām na kiṃcid bhu viduḥ labham tad niṣṭhāḥ tad gata dhiyaḥ tad karmāṇaḥ tad āśritāḥ vrata upavāsa nirata ahiṃsā ādi parivarjitāḥ sattāvān sarva bhūteṣu sa rudraḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ jaṃgama ajaṃgame yoma ātmani para tathā śayaḥ saṃprokta lakṣaṇa liṅgam kārayitvā atusthāpayet suvarṇa rajata ādyaiḥ tu satkṛtam vāsu dhātubhiḥ su pāṣāṇaiḥ sura naiśvamṛd ṭaṃmayam vā api śaktitas saḥ evam pūjitaḥ nityam dhyātaḥ ca eva maheśvari bhuṃjan gacchan tathā atiṣṭhan pārśva pṛṣṭhe tathā agratas jalaiḥ śubhaiḥ dhṛta ayaiḥ tunāḥ naiḥ ga adha anulepanaiḥ yat yat tat tat sadā prīṇayan satatam liṅgaiḥ marcayet mad parāyaṇaḥ mad kathāyām sadācittam saṃdhyāyet parameśvaram mad a bhairava ādyāḥ tu kathāḥ paurāṇa sambhavāḥ evam samarpita manāḥ puruṣaḥ umā parāyaṇaḥ param padam āpnoti jñā evam jñātvā anarodevīm ucyate bhava bandhanāt tat ananta phalam jñeyam saca ātmānam samuddharet etena eva upadeśena te ākhyātam mayā adhunā mānuṣāṇām hita arthāya saṃsārabha yad bhīruṇā kriyā yogaḥ tu vādya arthī dvayoḥ muktiḥ udāhṛtā kriyā yogam vinā ayogam duḥsādhyam amaraiḥ api yathā agniḥ tṛṇa jātāni daha ti anila saṃgāt tathā liṅga arcane bhāvaḥ udahet pāpāni aśeṣatas na vastra bhūṣaṇaiḥ ratnaiḥ na suvarṇasya rāśibhiḥ tuṣṭim yāti maheśānaḥ vinā bhaktim maheśvari iti etat kathita devyāḥ śaṃkareṇa purā mayā te kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi uvāca brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ vā ācarita vratāḥ mama etān pravakṣyāmi iti anena śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ mama tad dīkṣayā abhiyuktaḥ tvam bhūta pūrvaḥ mahā mune hi vyāptam hi vartate ca idam tat śṛṇuṣva yathātatham pṛthivī apaḥ tathā tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśaḥ eva ca sarvagaḥ śaśi sūryau ca śiva prakṛtayaḥ parāḥ sarve mantra ātmaka deva a mantra a vindu samāśritāḥ binduḥ nāda sthitaḥ nityam nādaśva paramātmani mantraiḥ taiḥ pūjyate devaḥ śivaḥ sarva mayaḥ mahān yakārasya aṣṭamam bījam mātrā dvādaśa bheditam akṣaram niratam rutvā ṣaḍaṅgam śivaiḥ mucyate dīrgha a dhaṃgāḥ samākhyāta athṛd stha avakra āṇi śūlinaḥ śivasya parama atyeṣā pūjā proktā manīṣibhiḥ evam evam jitam liṅgam sarva kāma phala pradam jñātavyaḥ su prayatnena dhyeyaḥ pūjyaḥ ca sarvadā prasādaḥ ume kṛtaḥ devi mantra ākhyānāt maheśvari prāsāda yena vikhyātam yāsyati iha mahī tale su kalābhiḥ samāyuktam na sa māheśvaraḥ bhavet ṇi devasya nityam saṃnihitāni ca tān vakṣyāmi iyaiḥ matraiḥ añcyate ca iha śūlinaḥ sadyojātam prapadyāmi sadyojātāya vai namaḥ dvipādau praṇava ādi samāyuktam namaskāreṇa saṃyutam mahā jyeṣṭha śva rudraśva kālarudraḥ tṛtīyakaḥ namaskāreṇa saṃyuktam dvitīyam parikīrtitam catuṣpādam samākhyātam namaskāreṇa saṃyutam maṃtrāṇām maṃtrarājam prakīrtitam heva tvam mānuṣa tvam ca gāndharva tvam ca rākṣasam tat sādhayet mantrī mantrarāja prabhāvāt striyaḥ dākṛṣṭāḥ śataśas uparāḥ ti na atra kāryā avicāraṇā devān daityān tathā asiddhān saṃyakṣa uraga rākṣasān bhūta vaitāla paiśācān vaśam ānayet mṛtyu bandha ārti bhaya dam duḥkhaṃgraha samudbhavam tad smaraṇāt mantrarājasya bhasmasāt yā ati nityaśas aikāhikam hi āhikam ca saṃjvaram cāturthikam tathā aghoram nāśayati āśu darśanāt sthāvaram jaṃgamam ca eva kṛtrimam dvipam hanti mantra prabhāvāt na saṃdehaḥ svarga mokṣam ca vidati iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām maṃtrarājaprabhāvaḥ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ evam prabhāvasya hi mantra rājñaḥ vidhānam uktam muninā apurāte tat brūhi naḥ sarvam aśeṣatas hitāya kāle yatataḥ narāṇām uvāca śṛṇudhvam etat munayaḥ sametāḥ sanatkumāreṇa vidhānam uktam su gupte su manoramet snātvā śuciḥ ca ekamanāḥ bhūtvā saṃsmṛtya mantram anasā tad aṅgaiḥ nyasam karābhyām karayoḥ cakuryāt hakāra yuktena tu vahninā paśvāt ṣaḍaṅgam guruṇā svareṇa aṣṭabhiḥ tu śikhā jñeyā aṣṭabhiḥ kavacam nyaset aṣṭabhiḥ netram uddiṣṭam phaḍustesam niyojayet māheśvaram vapus rutvā jaṭā mukuṭa bhūṣaṇam vāmadevāya jyeṣṭhāya namaḥ rudrāya ca namaḥ sarva ābharaṇa pūrṇa āgam candra ardha kṛta śekharam sva śarīram tatas pūjya puṣpa dhūpa vilepanaiḥ sthaṇḍile iva api liṅge iva apaścāt yajanam ārabhet om krāṃ thṛdayāya namaḥ hṛdayam āgneyyām nyaset om krīṃ aghorebhyaḥ śirase svāhā śiraḥ īśānyām nyaset oṃ ḍūṃ ghora ghoratarebhyaḥ śi khāyai vaṣaṭ śikhām nairṛtye vinyaset evam nyasya vidhānena hakāram vahni saṃyutam nādabindu kalā ākrāntam aghoram hṛdaye yajet madhye ghāreśvarī devīm tasya utsaṅge tu pūjayet aṃkuśaṃ kartarī dhvajau sa visargā aparā devī aghorā parikīrtitā ādi bījam samuddiśya dvitīyasya caturthakam trayodaśena ca ākrāntam vanhim ekādaśa anvitam aṣṭamasya ādimam rūpam samasta sya caturthakam huṃ phaṭkāreṇa saṃyutam eṣā avidyā mahāvidyā nāmnā aghoreśvarī iti ca tad sakāre pūjitā devī sadyas pratyaya kārakā evam saṃpūjaye devam aghoram ghora nāśanam kapāla mālā ābharaṇam catur bhujam vake kṣaṇam śūla dhara abhaya pradam trilocanam khaṇḍa śaśāṅka dhāriṇam dhyāyet haram yaḥ sa labheta īpsitam sarva avasthā gataḥ nityam yaḥ pūjayati śaṃkaram tasya pratyakṣa tām iyāt dadāti abhimata siddhim aṇima ādi guṇa ātmi kām tatas prasanna tām gatvā dehena anyena śaṃkaraḥ nayati abhīpsitān lokān ja rā mṛtyu vivarjitān madhu pattra guggulasya api guṭikābhiḥ samācaret japa homam vidhānena pātāle siddhim āpnuyāt satatam yaḥ japet mantram aghoram kleśa nāśanam tila homena naśyam tigraha pīḍā āyupadravāḥ sadā ghore śvarī devīm yaḥ japet arcayet naraḥ yaṃ yaṃ kāmam abhidhyāyan triṣu lokeṣu durlabham tam tam prāpnoti asaṃdigdham devyāḥ ca eva prabhāvāt badhvā aghoreśvarīm mudrām darśayet deva tuṣṭaye tām pravakṣyāmi vaḥ samyak sarva siddhi karām śubhām tau tu karau kṛtvā sva anyonyam granthayā iṅgulīḥ ubhayayoḥ tarjanībhyām tu saṃgṛhṇīyāt anāmike tayoḥ kṛtvā ati adhomukhām mudrām lalāṭe sam niveśayet tatas tatas siddhyam ti bhūta anisa deva asura mānuṣāḥ pralayam yāṃti te sarva maitrī sarva maitrī svacchaṃdasya mayā ākhyātam pūjanam diśi saṃsthitam liṅge vā sthaṇḍile vā api sarva kāma phala pradam dhīmahi om namaḥ śivāya aṣṭātriṃśe mahādevaḥ pañca brahma antara āśritaḥ maṃtu tathā avakam śṛṇudhvam ekacitayā īśānaḥ sarva vidyānām īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām sadya ādibhiḥ yajanti iha ye śivam sarva kāraṇam te mokṣam āpnuvanti iha mune yaḥ mokṣa kāṃkṣiṇaḥ prati īśāna ādi krameṇa eva īśānam arcayanti ye mayā ākhyātam ūrdhva vakram hita apasāḥ liṅga iva āsthaṃḍile śambhum sarva kāma phala āptaye iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām pañcabrahmākhyānam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca bhukti mukti karaḥ devaḥ śaṃkaraḥ parikīrtitaḥ jñānam mayā a muni śreṣṭha kim etat sakalam jagant jñānavān mohitaḥ daivāt mohaḥ māṃsam upāśritaḥ xcataḥ api na jānaṃti viṣṇu māyā vimohitāḥ patiṣyati etat sarvam samākhyā hi mānuṣāṇām hita arthāt sva karma vaśa gāḥ sarve prāṇinaḥ saṃbhavati atas maithunam ca sāmānyam etat sva pada ācarāṇām manasā atulyāḥ sva karma baddhāḥ prabhavaṃti nityam na yat kṛtena api yathā tathā api bhāvaḥ tadā jñānavatām narāṇām bhavanti yānti iha punar vināśam su saṃcaraṃtaḥ bahu duḥkha khinnāḥ kṛtvā iha pāpam niraye prayāṃti paścāt tathā amānuṣa tām ku yonim stavam na kurvati yadā asvadharmaiḥ yathā jale budruvat kṣaṇāt hi pañca brahma vidhānam tu mānuṣāṇām hita arthāt punar pṛcchāmi deveśaiḥ kathayasva prasādāt uvāca kathayāmi śṭaṇuṣva idam sarva siddhi pradāyakam bhaktāḥ iha amutra phala pradam kapilā pañcagavyena snātvā jatvā aṣṭakam naraḥ huyāt aṣṭa sāhasram tilaiḥ mucyeta pātakaiḥ tayā udakena saṃpūrya kumbham jamvā śatam śatam devasya dakṣiṇā amū teḥ japet ā astamanāt raveḥ aṣṭau eva sahasram tu hutvā sarva upapātakaiḥ kṛtvā hutvā nau vaśyā tām yānti yakṣa rākṣasa mānuṣāḥ maghu āca aṣṭa sahasram tu juhuyāt samidhaḥ tatas dadhi madhu ghṛta aktāḥ tu hutvā śāntiḥ bhavet iha kapilāyāḥ sa vatsāya dadhi ājya madhu saṃyutam guggulam ghṛta sammiśram hutvā ca aṣṭa sahasrakam sarve vaśyā bhavanti iha dutvā śata sahasrakam padma ādīni nidhānāni prāpnoti mucyate tathā hatyayā a brāhmaṇasya ihaśivasā yujyatām iyāt pradāpayet pañcagavya agniṣṭomasya tīrtha adbhiḥ sarvajātikam bhvāca aṣṭaśatam vidvāḥ vrajet kṣemī sadā pathini māditya abhimukhaḥ bhūtvā ūrdhvabāhuḥ śiva arcakaḥ brahmahatyā ādi pāpāni naśyati eva na saṃśayaḥ surā pānāt śarut mūtrāt steyāt sva guru dāragāt mucyate pātakāt sat yoniḥ āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ rājñām pratigṛhītvā ātu śūdra annam bahudhā atyadan gaja siṃha varāha iṣu śatru rāja kuleṣu vā manasā yaḥ japet mantram īśānam dhyānam āsthitaḥ prayāti paramam padam maṃtreṇa anena mām smaret iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām aṣṭātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca liṅgasya dakṣiṇāmūrteḥ māsam ekam tu yakṣiṇī samāgatya surūpa aṭyā sarvān kāmān prayacchati tat nāmnā astrī vaśam āyāti samarā trāt tad agratas karṇikārasya puṣpāṇām deva gandharva yoṣitaḥ samāgamya dadanti iṣṭam manasaḥ vatsara ardhāt sa lavaṇān tilān dutvā vaśam ānayate ripūn sa ghṛtena yaśaḥ kāmī sa dūrvaiḥ yāyuḥ eva ca mārjanena āmayān hanti sarṣapaiḥ akṣaṇam sadā candra sūrya uparāge tu japet aṣṭa sahasrakam liṅgasya dakṣiṇāmūrteḥ sa kāmān īpsitām labhet devasya dakṣiṇāmūrteḥ japet dā satatam sudhīḥ mita āśī yaḥ japet nityam mokṣam yāti na saṃśayaḥ sarve sattva avaśam īyuḥ śubhe madhu rakta puṣpaiḥ vaśe kārye kṛṣṇa puṣpaiḥ tu māraṇe tathā sarva pāpa labhet jīvaḥ saṃpūrṇasmin śarīrake sukham duḥkham vijānāti nidrā svapnam purā kṛtam mṛta śvā aham punar jāntaḥ jāta śvā aham punar mṛtaḥ nānā yoni sahasrāṇi mayā adṛṣṭāni jāyatā adhunā ajāta mātraḥ prāta saṃskāraḥ eva ca tatas śreyaḥ kariṣyāmi yena garbhena saṃbhavaḥ anveṣyāmi śiva jñānam saṃsāra vinivartakam evam sagarbha duḥkhena mahatā a paripīḍitaḥ mokṣa upāya viciṃtayan yathā giri vara ākrāntaḥ kaścid duḥkhena tiṣṭhati tathā jarāyuṇā dehī duḥkham tiṣṭhati veṣṭitaḥ patitaḥ sāgare yat duḥkham āste samākulaḥ na eva asti kutracid dehinām duḥkha bahulam su ghora mati saṃkaṭam iti etat su mahat duḥkham pāpinām parikīrtitam kevalam dharma buddhīnām samāsa udbhavāt sadā ca ikṣu vat pīḍyamānasya yantreṇa eva samantataḥ māna sya pāpa mudgarakeṇa ca yantreṇa pīḍitāḥ yadvat niḥsārāḥ syuḥ tilāḥ kṣaṇāt tathā śarīram niḥsāram yoni yantra nipīḍanāt rakta māṃsa mṛdā liptam viṣ mūtra dravya bhājanam vadana eka mahā dvāram gavākṣa aṣṭaka bhūṣitam jivhā argala anvitam bhoga tṛṣṇā āturam mūḍham rāga dveṣa vaśa anugam saṃvartita aṅga pratyaṅga añja rāyu pariveṣṭitam śata trayam ṣaṣṭi adhikam pañca peśī śatāni ca sārdhābhiḥ tisṛbhiḥ channam samantāt roma koṭibhiḥ śarīram sthūla sūkṣmābhiḥ dṛśya adṛśya āhitāḥ smṛtāḥ etāvatībhiḥ nāḍībhiḥ koṭibhiḥ tat samantataḥ dvātriṃśat daśanāḥ proktāḥ viṃśati śvanakhāḥ smṛtāḥ pittasya kuḍavam jñeyam kaphasya api āḍhakam tam māsa pala trayam mahāraktam majjā syāt ca caturguṇā madhu ardha kuḍavam jñeyam tat vījam dehinām balam raktam pala śatam jñeyam viṣ mūtram ca apramāṇāt hi śukra śoṇita saṃyogāt dehaḥ saṃjāyate yatas nityam viṣ mūtra saṃpūrṇaḥ tena ayam aśuciḥ smṛtaḥ yathā antar viṣṭhayā pūrṇaḥ śu ciḥsyāt na vahniḥ ghaṭaḥ śodhyamānaḥ hi dehaḥ yaḥ tena ayam aśuciḥ tatas tatra yatra api atipavitrāṇi pañcagavya havīṃṣi ca tatas hṛdyāni api anna pānāni yam prāpya surabhīni ca tvam prayānti āśu kim anyat aśuciḥ tatas he janāḥ kim na paśyaṃti yat niryāti dine dine sva dehāt kaśmalam pūti tad ādhāraḥ katham śuciḥ dehaḥ saṃśodhyamānaḥ api pañcagavya kuśa ambuṣu kapha mūtra purīṣa ādyaiḥ sa dehaḥ śudhyate katham śuciḥ ekaḥ pradeśaḥ api viṣ mūtrasya dṛteḥ iva spṛṣṭvā ātma deha srotāṃsi mṛd toyaiḥ śodhyate karaḥ tathā api aśuci bhāṃḍa syana virajyanti kiṃkarāḥ pāyaḥ su gandha puṣpa ādyaiḥ yatnena api susaṃskṛtaḥ ca śva puccha eva nāmitaḥ yathā jātyā eva ruṣṇaḥ ṛthaḥ śuklaḥ syāt tat u pāyāt saṃśodhyamānā api tathā bhavet mūrtiḥ na nirmalā aho mohasya māhātmyam yena idam vyāpitam jagant hīghram paśyan svakam doṣam kāyasya na virajyate dvayasya apagamāt śuddhiḥ śuddha sparśāt viśudhyati gaṅgā toyena sarveṇa mṛd bhāraiḥ parvata upamaiḥ mṛtyoḥ ācaret śau śudhyati tīrtha snānaiḥ tapobhiḥ vā aduṣṭa ātmā na eva śudhyati śva dṛtiḥ kṣālitā tīrthe kim śuddhim adhigacchati antarbhāva praduṣṭasya viśataḥ api hutāśanam samyak mṛd parvatena api atha bhāva duṣṭaḥ snāna paraḥ manuṣyaḥ na śuḍāti iti eva mayam vadāmaḥ prajvālya vanhim ghṛta taila siktam pradakṣiṇa āvarta śikham mahām tam gaṃgā ādi tīrtheṣu vasanti matsyāḥ devālaye pakṣi gaṇāḥ ca nityam bhāva ujhjhitāḥ tena phalam labhaṃte tīrtha avagāhāt ca tathā eva dānāt bhāva śuddham param śaucam pramāṇam sarva karmasu anyathā āliṃgya kāntā bhāvena duhitrī anyathā paśyadhvam asya bhāvasya mahābhāgyam aśeṣatas nārī abhāva hīnām na kāmayet nādyāt vividham annāyam bhakṣyāṇi surabhīni ca yadi cittam samādhatte cittam kāma ādiṣu triṣu bhāvāt śuci śuddha ātmā svarga mokṣam ca viṃdati bhāvena ekānta śuddhā ātmā adadat juvhan saced mṛtaḥ jñāna avāptyāḥ avāpa āśu lokān su bahu yājinām jñāna amala aṃnasa sāṃpusa sa dvairāgya mṛdā punar avidyā rāga viṣ mūtra lepa gandha viśodhanam tvac mātra sāra niḥsāra kadalā sāra saṃnibham jñātvā evam doṣa dehayaḥ prājñaḥ sa śithilaḥ bhavet sā utikrāmati saṃsāram dṛḍha grāhī ca tiṣṭhati evam e tat mahā kaṣṭam janma duḥkham prakīrtitam puṃsām ajñāna doṣeṇa nānā karma vaśena ca śloka arthena tu vakṣyāmi yat uktam grantha koṭibhiḥ bahavaḥ api hi rājānaḥ param mokṣam itas gatāḥ niḥ mama iti mama iti evam baddhāḥ śata sahasraśas saṃmūcchitasya duḥkhena yoni yantra nipīḍanāt moha saṃjñena dehinaḥ sṛṣṭa mātrasya ghoreṇa jvaraḥ samupajāyate saṃmūḍhasya smṛti bhraṃśaḥ śīghram saṃjāyate punar ratiḥ saṃjāyate tūrṇa jantoḥ tatra eva janmani raktaḥ mūḍhaḥ ca lokaḥ yat na kārye saṃpravarta te naca ātmānam vijānāti na param na ca daivatam na śṛṇoti param śreyaḥ sati cakṣuṣi na īkṣate saṃsāre kliśyate tena garva lobha vaśa anugaḥ avyakta iṃdriya vṛtti tvāt vālye duḥkham mahat punar pīḍā bālagrahaiḥ api viṣ mūtra bhakṣaṇa ādi añcamohāt dālaḥ samācaret haumāre karṇapīḍāyām mātā pitrā ūśva sādhane syāt guru tāḍane pravṛta indriya vṛtti tvāt kāma rāga prapīḍanāt kāma agni pariveditaḥ strī pumān śukra vidavaḥ pāma nasya ca kaṇḍūyana agni tāpena yat bhavet strīṣu tad vidaḥ yādṛśam manyate saukhyam gaṇḍepūya vinirgamāt tādṛśam strī puṃs antavyam na adhikam tāsu vidyate bhavati tādṛśam strīṣu vijñeyam mūḍhaiḥ kalpitam anyathā tat tat tat tat tat sarva doṣa āśrayāsu ca na aṇu mātram sukham tā su kathitam pañcacūḍayā vigraham sarva kriyāsu aśaktim ca jarayā jarjarīkṛtam tat tat tat tat tat tat apūrvavat svam ātmānam jarayā aparivartitam xchā abhibhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ patnī putra ādi bāndhavaiḥ aśakta tvāt na ādriyate bhṛtyaiḥ ca paribhūyate aśaktaḥ sādhitum tasmāt yuvā dharma samācaret iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām saṃsāracikitsāvarṇanam nāma dvicatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca kutsitam yoṣit arthe ya striyā uktam pañcacūḍayā strīṇām svabhāva vakṣyāmi śṭaṇu vipra yathātatham striyaḥ mūlam hi doṣāṇām laghu cittāḥ sadā mune atra api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam nāradasya ca saṃvādam puṃścalyā āpam cacūḍayā lokān paricaran dhīmān devarṣiḥ nāradaḥ purā dadarśa apsarasam vāhmīm pañcacūḍām anuttamām śrī nāradā uvāca strīṇām svabhāvam icchāmi tvattaḥ śrotum sumadhyame pratyuvācana śakya astrī sanī vainiṃditum khiyā mataḥ namām arhasi deva ṛṣa niyoktum prabham īdṛśam tām uvāca atha devarṣiḥ satyam vada sumadhyame mṛṣāvāde bhavet doṣaḥ satye doṣaḥ na vidyate iti uktā a sākṛta mati rabhasā a cāru hāsinī strī doṣān śāśvatān satyān bhāṣitum saṃpracakrame vāca tiṣṭhati sa doṣaḥ strīṣu nārada striyaḥ mūlam hi pāpānām tathā tvam api vettha samājñāta anarthavataḥ pratirūpa an vaśe sthitām n patīn antaram āsādya na ālam bhāryāḥ pratīkṣitum bhajāmahe tat tat tat tat tat eva incchanti yoṣitaḥ anathim tvāt manuṣyāṇām bhayāt parijanasya ca maryādāyām amaryādāḥ striyaḥ tiṣṭhati bhartṛṣu niśvayaḥ na bhayāt na api anukrośāt na artha hetoḥ kathaṃcana na jñāti kula sambandhā triyaḥ tiṣṭhati bhartṛṣu yauvane vartamānānām ṭaṣṭa ābharaṇa vāsasām nārīṇām svaira vattīnām spṛhayati kulastryaḥ te dayitāḥ striyaḥ arpitāḥ saṃprasajrjate kula andha jaḍa vāmane maguṣu apica devarṣeye ca anye kutsitā narāḥ strīṇām agamyaḥ lokeṣu na asti kaścid mahā mune alābhāt puruṣāṇām ca bhayāt pari janasya ca cala svabhāva a dus sevya a durgātya abhāvāt tathā mājñasya puruṣasya e ha yathā vāsaḥ tathā striyaḥ na agniḥ tṛpyati kāṃṣṭhānām na āpagānām mahā udadhiḥ tathā sarva bhūtānām na puṃsām vāma locanāḥ sarva bhūtānām na puṃsām vāma locanāḥ dṛṣṭvā eva puruṣa hṛdyam yoniḥ prakliyatetriyaḥ puruṣa dṛṣṭvā sugandham mala varjitam yoniḥ praklidyateḥ trīṇām dṛteḥ pādāt iva udakam kāmānām apidātāram kāmānām mānasāṃtvayoḥ rakṣitāram na mṛṣyanti bhartāram paramam striyaḥ saṃcayāt antakaḥ śamanaḥ mṭatyuḥ pātālam vaḍavāmukham kṣura dhārā viṣam sarpaḥ vanhiḥ iti ekatas striyaḥ yatas ca bhūtāni mahant ti paṃca yatas ca lokaḥ vihitaḥ vidhātrā yatas pumāṃsaḥ pramadā aśva nirmitāḥ tadā eva doṣaḥ pramadā su nāradaiḥ uvāca mā mā aimānavālokeḥ strīṣu sajjanti abhīkṣṇaśas mohena parama āviṣṭāḥ daiva ādiṣṭena bāliśāḥ katham āsām narāḥ saṃgam kurvan ti satatam mune durjayam kāmena anirjitaḥ kaścid tiṣṭhati iha mahī tale etat brūhi mune samyak nārīṇām ceṣṭitam punar yaḥ dharmaḥ yaḥ paurvikī saṃjñā upacāraḥ kriyā vidhiḥ yathādṛṣṭam bhagavān pratra aṣṭāvakrasya saṃvādi śaya asahayat purā mā āsīt tat śṛṇu kāleya pravakṣyāmi yathā tathā anvitām madānyasya prabhām nāma sādhum cāritra bhūṣaṇām ha mutām dadmi diśam saṃdrakṣyase yadi tathā idānīm mahā kāryam vaktum arhati mama bhavān kim draṣṭavyam mayā tatra yathā vakṣyati mām bhavān uvāca rudrasya āyatanam dṛṣṭvā asiddha cāraṇa sevitam tapasvinīm mahābhāgām vṛddhām dīkṣām anuṣṭhitām draṣṭavyā asā tvayā tatra saṃpūjyā ca eva yatnatas tām dṛṣṭvā vinivṛttaḥ stvam prāṇi grā grahīṣyasi yadi eṣa samayaḥ satyaḥ sādhyatām gamyatām iti uvāca yatra tvam vakṣyase sādho uta trayāsyāmi asaṃśayam tathā atusādhayiṣyāmi bhavān bhavatu satya vāc himavantam giri śreṣṭham siddha cāraṇa sevitam gatvā aprāpa nadīm puṇyām bāhudām puṇya vāhinīm tatra asau vidhi nānā tva āśa yanesau vāsaha snātvā prātar atha utthāya rudrāṇīkūpam āvrajat mandākinīṃ dhaneśasya rakṣitā aṅgutyakaiḥ sadā vaiśravaṇaḥ yamaiḥ āyāti tvām draṭum ṛṣi sattamaiḥ bhuvanam praviśa tvam mama yathākāmam su satkṛtaḥ pādya arghena āsanena eva pūjābhiḥ tam apūjayat tava ājñayā amune sarvāḥ ānṛtyeran puṃścalīḥ iha mad ātithyam paramam kāryam bhavataḥ vāḍham iti asau tatas varā ghṛtācī camiśrakeśī tathā urvaśī rambhā tvalaṃbusā citrā viśvāciḥ ca manoharā sukeśī mumukhī ca eva hāsinī caratipriyā etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca nṛtye yurvādyāni vividhāni ca yaśva gandharvāḥ ṛṣeḥ tu puratas niśam nṛtyam sāgraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ jātaḥ sāṃpratam karavāṇi kim sarvam ājñāpyatām iti atha tuṣṭa stutam prāha pūjitaḥ asmi dhaneśvaraiḥ hirasā atas namaskṛtya tāra uttarā mukhaḥ tat samena bhūmi bhāgena yā voḍhavyāni aśeṣatas tatra āśrama padam ramyam aṣṭāvakraḥ udadarśa saḥ śailān ca vividhān tatra hema ratna mayān śubhān maṇi ratna mayīm bhūmipuṣkariṇyaḥ anyāni api su ramyāṇi mahā ṛṣeḥ bhāvitātmanaḥ dadarśa adbhuta saṃkāśam sarva ratna mayam gṛham mahantaḥ tatra vividhāḥ kāñcanāḥ parvata uttamāḥ tad mūrdhani cavi mānāni ramyāṇi apsarasā aṅgaṇaiḥ mandāra puṣpa saṃkīrṇā ati tra mandākinī nadī svayam prabhāva amaṇayaḥ vacaiḥ bhūmiḥ su bhṛṣitā nānāvidha aiśva bhavanaiḥ maṇi ratna vibhūṣitaiḥ muktā jāla parikṣitaiḥ vicitra maṇi toraṇaiḥ ṛṣiḥ samaṃtataḥ upaśyat saṃvṛtam parva śubham nānā rūpāḥ saptamune gṛhāt tasmāt viniryayuḥ manoramāḥ manoharā yām yām prapaśyet kanyām sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitām saca tāsām mu rūpāṇām praviveśa gṛrha dvijaḥ tatra apaśyat śubhām kanyām sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitām tatra apaśyat śubhām kanyām sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitām ratna paryakam āsīnām viraja umbara dhāriṇīm pratyutthāya ca tam vipram sādhvī tu abhyavadat tadā prāha vismaya anvitaḥ yā a prasannā a śubha ācārā ekā mām anutiṣṭhatu śeṣāḥ svān ālayān yān tu viśrameham sukham ca yat atha tāḥ tam ṭaṣim natvā yayuḥ sarvāḥ svam ālayam saṃyutā mad bhūtvā paryacara brāhmaṇaṃśaṃsita vratam tām saṃviśan prāha rajani iti ativartate dvitīye śayane divye tathā vipreṇa bhāṣitā saṃlāpāt tena vipreṇa saṃviveśa mahā prabho atha sā avepamāna aṅgā śayanam tu adhirohatām vyapadiśya mahā ṛṣeḥ vainimittam śītajam tadā svāgata svāgatam ca astutam ṭaṣi muni sattamam tam bhagavantam abhāṣata nirvikāra mṛṣi dṛṣṭvā kāṣṭha loṣṭha upamam tadā duḥkhi tāṃtrekṣya saṃjalpam akārṣīt ṛṣiṇā saha pāmena mohitā aca aham strīṇām puruṣāt dhṛtiḥ brahman na kāmakāra ustitām prahṛṣṭaḥ bhava viprarṣe kāmātarhi bhṛśam tvayi prārthitaḥ darśanāt eva bhajamānām bhajasva mām sarvān kāmān vidhāsyāmi sarva kāma phala pradā tvad vaśā abhaviṣyām iram asaha sarvān kāmān upāśnānaḥ ye divyāye ca mānuṣāḥ na atas param hi nārīṇām kārya kiṃcana vidyate apipāṃśubhiḥ uvāca para dārān aham bhadrena gaccheyam kathaṃcana dūṣitam dharmaśāstreṣu para dāra abhimarśanam bhadre nirveṣṭu kā mam mām viddhi satyena te śape mad putra artha kila saṃtatiḥ evam lokān gamiṣyāmi putraiḥ iti na saṃśayaḥ aha priyaḥ strīṇām yathā kāmaḥ rati śīla ahi yoṣitaḥ sahasrāya eka tām nārīm prāpnoti iha kadācana tathā śata sahasreṣu yaṭikā acit pativratā na etāḥ jānaṃti pitaram nakulam naca mātaram loṭayanti kulaṃnāryaḥ kūlāni iva saridvarāḥ doṣān amanda mandāsu prajāpatiḥ abhāṣata chandāt kivākārya vadasva mama sa astrī provāca bhagavant drakṣya se deśa kālāt tathā sarpiḥ abhiprekṣya striyam tām jarayā nvitām na aramat tatra tatra āsya dṛṣṭi rūpa parājitā devatā iyam gṛhasya asya śāpāt nūnam virūpitā mayā agamat tad ahar śeṣam manasā a vyākulena tu rūpam saṃdhyā abhra saṃyuktam kim upasthāpyatām tava tadā tān trīn trāna udakam iha ānaya upāsiṣyet atas saṃdhyām vāgyataḥ niyata iṃdriyaḥ divya tailam upādāya strāna śāṭīm upānayat tā ca muninā asau strī tena mahātmanā atha āsya tailena aṅgāni sarvāṇi eva asya ślakṣṇayat hanta ca ānmārjitam tatra snāna śālām upānayat bhadrāsanam tatra citram ṛṣiḥ anvāviśat navam tathā upaviṣṭam prayatā tasmin bhadrāsane śubhā trāpayāmāsa śanais tam ṭaṣi mukha hasta vat ha vyatītām rajanīm kṛtsnām na jajñau saḥ mahā manāḥ pūrvasyām diśi somam ca saḥ paśyat uditam divi atha upāsya sahasrāṃśum kim karomi iti uvāca tām sā ca amṛta rasa prakhyam ṛṣeḥ annam upānayat tasya svādu tayā anna syana prabhūtam cakāra saḥ vyagamat ca api tatas saṃdhyā agamat punar sātadātena vipreṇa tathā vṛtyā anivartitā svatantrā smi iti uvāca aṣṭāvakrā uvāca na asti svatantra tā strīṇām asvatantrāḥ hi yoṣitaḥ bhūmau nipatamānāyāḥ śaraṇam mama bhava anaghaiḥ yat iva a doṣa jātam tvam para dāreṣu paśyasi mānam sparśayāmi aya pāṇi gṛhṇīṣva mama dvijaiḥ svatantrām mām vijānīhi yaḥ adharmaḥ saḥ stuvai mayi uvāca harantī doṣa jātāni naram yātu yathecchakam taraṃsye para dāreṣu bhadre svam śayanam vraja uvāca tathā asti loka ihi kācid strī yām vai svātaṃtryam arhati kumāra vimatim vipra śraddhām naḥ vijihīhi me uvāca ha jijñāsā iyam mṛṣeḥ tasya vighnam satyam tu kim bhavet bhavet divya ābharaṇa vastrā hi kanyā iyam mām upasthitā kiṃtu asyāḥ paramam rūpam jīrṇam āsīt kathaṃcana vṛtteḥ uvāca katham nivṛttaḥ bhagavān tat ravītu mahā mune aṣṭāvakraḥ nvapṛcchat tām rūpam vikuruṣe katham anṛtam ca na vaktavyam brūhi brāhmaṇa kāmyayā uvāca mātrā eṣā akāmyā brāhmaṇa sattama śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ sarva yat idam satya vikramaiḥ uttarām mām diśam vid vidṛṣṭam strī cāpalam cate hi jijñāsā iyam prayuktā āme sthirīkartu te anagha thavirāṇām api strīṇām ca maithuna ujvaraḥ tuṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ te sa vāsavāḥ bhaviṣyati tām kanyām prāpsyasi tām vipra putriṇī sā bhaviṣyati bhavat tvam me tatas vyāhṛtam uttaram taiḥ lokaiḥ tribhiḥ sadā yāvat ravīmi viprarṣe aṣṭāvakra yathātatham tava hetoḥ dvijarṣabha tasya saṃmānana artham etvayi vākyam prabhāṣitam śrutvā tu vacanam tasyāḥ sa vipraḥ prāñjaliḥ tadā anujñātaḥ tayā ca api sva gṛham punar āviśat gṛham āgamya viśrāntaḥ sva janam pratipūjyam ca pṛṣṭaḥ ca tena vipreṇa dṛṣṭam etat nidarśanam antarātmanā tayā ca aham anu prakīrtitaḥ śrāvita śva asmi tad vākyam gṛham ca abhyāgataḥ prabho tatas vipraḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva mesutaiḥ aṣṭāvakraḥ tathā iti uktvā pratigṛtya catāṃśubhām yām parama dharma ātma aprītimān ca bhavat tadā kanyām tām pratijagrāha bhā parama śobhanām mā as sa dānāya bhavati ekā pativratā yasyāḥ saṃkīrtanāt sadyas sarva pāpa kṣayaḥ bhavet narāḥ keli īdṛśāḥ nityam yeṣām saṃkīrtanāt kaliḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām tricatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ punar anyat tu vakṣyāmi caḥ asatī tve yathā strīṇām tat śṛṇuṣva mahā mune tathā atithi gṛhasthānām nṛpa ādīnām dvijottamāḥ ete syuḥ yadi saṃtuṣṭāḥ brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ bhavanti sukhinaḥ nityam devāḥ indra purogamāḥ iha āmiḥ dharma kāmānām paratra ca śubhā āgatiḥ atas samīkṣitaḥ asmābhiḥ satyam asti iha yoṣi tām māyā mūrkha tvam ati lobha tā aśaucam nirdaya tvam ca strīṇām doṣāḥ svabhāva jāḥ śrūyante yoṣitaḥ kāścid sattva dharme samāsthitāḥ dvijāḥ tathā sva karma sthāḥ gṛhiṇaḥ gṛhakarmaṇi rāja ānotha viśa śvāpi prajā pālana tatparāḥ arundhatī vasiṣṭhasya prakhyātā supativratā tad rūpam na cakāra pativratā svāhā ca eva api tām dṛṣṭvā a purā vismaya mā agamat dhanyā tvam asi kalyāṇi yā tvam ekā pativratā maham kartum śaktā ca anyā kariṣyati tasmāt tvayā āḥ striyaḥ kā śvit prekṣiṣyanti su bhāvāt bhartuḥ dvija agni saṃnidhau sukham tāsām dhanam putrāḥ tu avaidhavyam bhaviṣyati abhimantavyā aguṇaiḥ yuktā pativratā gacchāma utas vayam praṣṭum strīṇām pativratām tatas dadṛśuḥ āyānta sva dhāmnaḥ ghṛta kumbhakām arundhatīm pati prāṇām pateḥ priya hita īratām tasthuḥ agre tasya astu vartmani tatas sā tān mudā dṛṣṭvā jñātvā devān arundhatī pradakṣiṇam upāvṛtya praṇipatya punar punar tat śrutvā vacaḥ tasyāḥ pra ūcuḥ tām varavarṇinīm praṣṭum vayam samāyātāḥ kaṃcid praśnam hinaḥ vada sācatānāha medhā agni viśrama dhva kṣaṇāt anu tat sarva praśnam ceṣṭitam ātmanaḥ yāvat āyāmi saṃgṛtya jala pūrṇam imam ghaṭam bharan tat śrutvā vāḍha tān āha pūrayadhvam imam ghaṭam uvāca tapasā abrahmacaryeṇa svargāt mām cyāvayiṣyati uvāca brāhmaṇāḥ prītyāḥ nityam saṃgṛhītaḥ mahā asuraiḥ uvāca yāvat rahaḥ nava astrīṇām yāvat na eva abhibhāṣaṇam tāvat tāsām satī tvam syāt tasmāt rakṣyāḥ vara striyaḥ pādaḥ kumbhasya pūryatām iti ukte jala saṃpūrṇa kumbhe devāḥ bruvan tatas iti catuścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ kārayet paśvāt vidhivat vija puṃgavaiḥ tatas saṃpūjayet viprān sa patnīkān mahā mune tatas kṣamāpayet viprān imam mantram udāharet yathā madra īśa duhitrī ayam ātmānuvatī varān iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām paṃcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ adya api saṃśayaḥ iti ekaḥ kālacakram prati prabho mṛtyu cinham yathā devaiḥ kim pramāṇam tathā āyuṣaḥ hariḥ uvāca satyam te kathayiṣyāmi yena kālaḥ prabudhyate ahar pakṣam tathā māsam mṛtum ca ayana vatsaram tat te iham saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta tvena suṃdari akasmāt pāṇḍuram deham ūrdhva rāgam samaṃtataḥ tadā amṭatyum vijānīyāt ṣaṣ māsa abhyantaram priye ṣaṣ māsa abhyantaram mṛtyuḥ jñātavyaḥ kāla vedibhiḥ kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇam sarpasaḥ tam ca ṣaṣ māsam jīvitam tathā ulmīlayanti gātrāṇi tālukam śuṣyate yadā hi jīvitam tu tadā tasya māsam ekam na saṃśayaḥ sthūlā jivhā kliyanti bhāmini ṣaṣ māsāt jāyate mṛtyuḥ cinhaiḥ taiḥ upalakṣayet bhavatena yat ātmānam vikṛtam sthūlam eva ca ṣaṣ māsa āyūḥ sa vijñeyaḥ kālacakram vijānatā śiraḥ hīnām yadā achāyām svakīyām upalakṣayet athavā achāyayā ahīnam māsam ekam na jīvati māṃgikāḥ kathitāḥ bhadraiḥ iva atyasthān śṛṇu sāṃpratam raśmi hīnam yadā devi soma arka maṇḍala dvayam dṛśyate paṭala ākāram māsa ardhena vipadyate arundhatī mahāyānam indu lāñchana varjitam arundhatī mahāyānam indu lāñchana varjitam tat upi jīvati varṣa ardha tathā vā adṛṣṭa tārakaḥ dṛṣṭe gṛhe ca diś mohaḥ ṣaṣ māsāt jāyate dhruvam gṛdhra kākaiḥ śva ṣaṣ māsa āyuḥ na saṃśayaḥ ṛṣayaḥ svarga pathī na eva dṛśyeta ca ambare ṣaṣ māsa āyuḥ vijānīyāt puruṣaiḥ kāla vedibhiḥ akasmāt rāhuṇā grastam sūrya vāsas mama eva ca tat paśyet ṣaṣ māsān triyate sphuṭam makṣikaiḥ nīla varṇa ābhaiḥ a kasmāt veṣṭyate pumān jīvatā māsam ekam tu jñātavyam paramārthāt gṛdhaḥ kākaḥ kapota śvaśiraḥ ca ākramya tiṣṭhati māsa ekena na saṃśayaḥ evam ca ariṣṭa bhedaṃtubātya stham samudāhṛtam hita arthāya saṃkṣepeṇa vadāmi aham vāmam śuklam vijānīyāt dakṣiṇam kṛṣṇa saṃjñitam dakṣiṇam sūryam ityāḥ durvāmacandraudāhṛtaḥ śuciḥ bhūtvā smaret evam susrātaḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kara oru tvāt mṛgayet ca śubha aśubham kaniṣṭhām kaniṣṭhām kaniṣṭhā āditas kṛtvā yāvat aṅguṣṭha kampri ye sampuṭa ākāra hastau tu pūrvāḥ di mukha saṃsthitaḥ smaret nava arṇakam mantrya avadaṣṭa uttaram śatam tasmin parvaṇi te dekhā dṛśyate bhṛṅga saṃnibhā tad tithau mṛtyuḥ vijñeyaḥ kṛṣṇe śukle tathā apriye niśvitam maraṇam tasya kālacakrasya kīrtitam adhunā anāda jam vakṣye saṃkṣepāt kāla lakṣaṇam gama āgamam viditvā tu karma kuryāt śṛṇu priye jñātvā tu tatvāt kṣaṇam truṭiḥ lava ca eva nimepam kāṣṭha kālikam evam saṃharate kālaḥ paripāṭyā sadāśivaḥ ṛtuḥ vikāraiḥ bhūtāḥ ca guṇaḥ tatra eva bhāmini pramāṇam dakṣiṇam proktam jñātavyam prāṇa vedibhiḥ bhūta saṃkhyām yadā prāṇaḥ vahate ca eḍa ādayaḥ varṣa trayam tadā tasya jīvitasya na saṃśayaḥ na ādaśa pravāhena dvau abdāni sa jīvati pañcadaśa pravāhena abdam ekam gata āyuṣaḥ tathā tu pañcaviṃśat dinānām tu vahatā vāma nāḍikā hi jīvitam tu tadā tasya māsa traya gata āyuṣaḥ ṣaḍviṃśat dina mānena māsa dvaya gatāḥ yuṣaḥ dinānām māsam ekam samākhyātam jīvitam vāma gocare yam vāma vāyu pramāṇāt anupūrvaśas catuḥ sthāne sthitā devi ṣoḍaśā etāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām pramāṇam vakṣyāmi adhunā ahi hita arthāt ṣar̤a dināni āditas kṛtvā saṃkhyāyāḥ ca yathāvidhi atas etat antargatam kālam vāma randhra itra kāśitam ha ṣaṣ dināni yad ārūḍham varṣa dvayam sa jīvati māsāni aṣṭau vijānīyāt dināni aṣṭādaśa ani tu prāṇaḥ sapta dine devi varṣa dvayam na saṃśayaḥ sapta māsān vijānīyāt dinaiḥ ṣaḍtiḥ gata āyuṣaḥ māsām catvāri vijñeyam caturviṃśat dina avadhi tat tri māsakam māsa dvayam ca dve māsa dina dvādaśa kī ti tāḥ pūrvavat kathitāya tu kālam teṣām na pūrvake ekādaśa pravāhena varṣame kaṃna jīvati māsa anava tathā prokta ādinā aṣṭa dina avadhi dvādaśa ahe pravāhena varṣam ekam gata āyuṣam māsān sata vijānī yāt dina ṣaṭum udāhṛtam hata nāḍī trayodaśa dina avadhi tasya māsa aśva tvāri kīrtitāḥ prāṇavāhaḥ yadā āvāme caturdaśa dināni dvādaśā pravāhena dvi māsam jīvitam khalu antarāla daśā antare tṛtīyam ca samāsena kālacakram vadāmi aham ṣoḍaśa aha pravāhena nava māsaiḥ gata āyuṣam aṣṭādaśa tatra kathitam sādhaka īśvaraiḥ aṣṭādaśa dina avadhi jīvitam aṣṭa māsam tu dināḥ dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ caturviṃśat dināḥ tatra niśvayena avadhāraya prāṇavāhaḥ yadā āvāme trayoviṃśat dina avadhi māsāḥ catvāraḥ vijñeyāḥ ṣa dināni tathā uttare caturviṃśa pravāhena māsa trayam sa jīvati dināḥ tatra daśa aṣṭa ca saṃharati avicārāt avāntara dina āyetu saṃkṣepāt prakaṭīkṛtāḥ vāma cāram samākhyātam dakṣiṇam śṛṇu sāṃpratam jīvati triṃśa vāha pravāhena pañca ahena vinaśyati tadā atasya jīvita syana saṃśayaḥ dakṣiṇam kathitam prāṇam madhyastham kathayāmi te iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām kālajñānam nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ kathitam tu tvayā devaiḥ kāla jñānam yathārthāt tu saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ hi vartate sarva jantuṣu yathā ca asyana mṛtyuḥ cavam catekālam āgatam uvāca śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi iyat tvayā apṛcchata iti aham kathayāmi samāsena mānuṣāṇām hita arthāt pṛthivī apaḥ tathā tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam eva ca mṛtyoḥ durjaya tā mukkā śabdabrahma vicakṣaṇaiḥ eteṣām hi samāyogaḥ śarīram pāñcabhautikam mahā brahmā sarveṣām sarva gaḥ sthitaḥ tu vilīyaṃte saṃbhavanti punar tatas tathā yatnāt tapas mantra balāḥ yadi śvetam nayan ati ati ghora rūpaḥ kālaḥ karālaḥ tridiva īśa nātha dagdhaḥ tvayā tvam punar eva tuṣṭaḥ stotraiḥ stutvā tvām prakṛtim sa lebhe tvayā asaca uktaḥ kṛpayā ajanānām adṛṣṭa rūpaḥ pracariṣyasi iti dṛṣṭam tvayā tat nihitam mayā ahi prabho varāt te punar utthitam ca śambhuḥ tām āha śaśi vadane yoginaḥ ye kṣayanti kālam jātam sakalam anaghāḥ tat śṛṇuṣva ekacittā uvāca pañcabhūta ātmakaḥ dehaḥ sadā yuktaḥ tu guṇaiḥ tejaḥ vai jāyate māt hi pṛthivī bhavet pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni gacchanti kramaśas varam dharā pañcaguṇā proktā apaḥ ca eva caturguṇāḥ śabdaka guṇam ākāśam pṛthivī ādiṣu kīrtitāḥ maḥ śabdaḥ sparśaḥ varūpam ca rasaḥ gandhaḥ ca pañcamaḥ vijahāti guṇam svam svam tadā bhūtam vipadyate yadā āguṇam vigṛhṇāti prādurbhūtam tat ucyate tasmāt viyoginā anityam sva kāya ākāśa jāḥ guṇāḥ mācintanīyāḥ prayatnena devi kāla jigīṣuṇā kāmyayā śraddadhānāya dātavyam bhakti yuktāya dhīmate tad anāstikāya śuddhāya dharma nityāya bhāmini ha śayyāyām yogam yuṃjīta yoga vid dīpam vinā andhakāre tu prajāsu mama etu dhārayet tarjanyā api hitau karṇau pīḍayitvā amuhūrtakam tasmāt saṃśrūyate śabdaḥ tum vanhi samudbhavaḥ sarva rogam nihanti āśu jvarāyu padravān bahūn upalakṣayet nityam ekānte ghaṭikā dvayam jitvā amṭatyum yathākāmam sva icchayā paryaṭet iha yathā abhnat atenādam prāvṛṣ nabhasi saṃsthitam tam śrutvā mucyate saṃsāra bandhanāt tatas sa yogibhiḥ nityam sūkṣmaḥ sūkṣmataraḥ bhavet palālam iva dhānya arthī iti ajet vandham aśeṣatas hi śabdabrahma edam prāpya ye kecid anya kāṃkṣiṇaḥ muṣṭinā hi jñātvā aparam idam brahma sukha dam mukti kāraṇam kāla pāśena mṛtyu pāśa vaśaṃgatāḥ nidrā ālasyam mahā vighnam jitvā āśacam prayatnāt śata vṛddhaḥ pumān labdhvā yāvat āyuṣyam abhyaset gṛtyuṃjaya vapus stambhaḥ ārogyam ca āyus vardhanam mantraḥ api na eva bīja naca akṣaram tam tad an ahaṃtam an uccārya śabda brahma param śivam tasmāt śabda anava proktāḥ prāṇa tu lakṣitāḥ tathā bhṛṃ gaṃghaṃṭā vīṇā ādi vaṃśakam dundubhiḥ śaṅkha śabdaḥ cana maṃ megha garjitam mad mad samāśrayet dhyāya navam sadā yogī puṇya pāpaiḥ na lipyate māse ca tat aṃvi ke mriyate bhyasyamānaḥ tam yogī tiṣṭhe ddivāniśam sarva vyādhi haram nādam vaśyā ākarṣaṇam uttamam dvitīyam nadate kāṃsyam staṃbhaya iti āṇinām gatim sarva bandhayet na atra tṛtīyam nadate śṛṅgam abhicāre niyojayet tu vadate paraḥ mama śvaraḥ abhuvi yakṣa yakṣa gandharva kanyā aśvatasya aṣṭādaśa ati hi yathā īpsitām mahā asi dvi yoginaḥ kāmatas pi vā vīṇā tu pañcamaḥ nādaḥ śrūyate yogibhiḥ sadā tat yat iva śa nādam sarvajña tvam prajāyate dundubhi dhyāyamānaḥ tu jarā mṛtyu vivarjitaḥ śaṅkha śabdena deveśikā rūpam prapadyate sarva jñaḥ sarva darśī ca kāmarūpī vrajati asau etat te sarvam ākhyātam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi uvāca tat kālam jigamiṣoḥ samyak vāyoḥ liṅgam yathā bhavet tena jñātvā dinam yogī prāṇāyāma paristhitaḥ sa jayati āgatam kālam mām sārdhena eva sundari hṛd sthaḥ vāyuḥ sa dāvaḥ sa unupāvakaḥ sarva gataḥ mahān jñāna vi jñānam utsāham sarva vāyoḥ pravartate dhāraṇāyām sadā ātiṣṭhet jarā mṛtyu jighāṃsayā lohakāraḥ yathā bhastrā māpūrya mukhatas nyatas yaḥ pi sarvam āvṛtya saḥ ugre tiṣṭhat daśa aṅgulam tris paṭhet āya prāṇāyāmaḥ saḥ ucyate gatvā gatvā nivartate candra sūrya ādayaḥ grahāḥ adya api na nivartate prāṇāyāma parāyaṇāḥ madhu pibet dijaḥ tat āpnoti phalam devī prāṇānām dhāraṇā ekayā tasmāt dvijaḥ kalyam utthāya prāṇāyāma ekam ācaret sadā ekānte prāṇāyāma paraḥ bhavet mṛtyum vinirjitya vāyu gaḥ khecarī iti saḥ siddhasya bhavaterūpam kāntiḥ medhā parākramaḥ śauryam vāyu samaḥ gati āsaukhyam ślāghyam surā ādibhiḥ etat kathitam aśeṣam vāyoḥ siddhi yadā adbhutam yogī śiśira viyuktyā atejaḥ prakāśayet madhya mede tāram tāram paśyeyāyet muhūrta ardha tam eka bhāvaḥ api śvetam raktam tathā pītam kṛṣṇam indrāyudha prabham tam viditvā tu kāmāṅgī krīḍate kāma rūpadhṛk praveśanam aṇima ādi guṇa avāptiḥ manasā ca avalokanam dūrāt śravaṇa vijñānam adṛśyam bahu rūpadhṛk mad adhyayana saṃpanna nānā śāstra viśāradāḥ jñāninaḥ pi vimutyante pūrva karma vaśa anugāḥ paśyaṃtaḥ apina paśyaṃti śṛṇvānāḥ badhirāḥ yathā yathā andhā mānuṣe loke mūḍhāḥ pāpa vimohitāḥ yat aham etam puruṣam mahāṃtama ā ditya varṇa tamasaḥ parastāt tam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ pathī vidyate prāpaṇāya kālam jitvā yathāyogī ca amara tvam prapadyate punar parataram vakṣye yathā mṭatyuḥ na jāyate turīyāt devi bhūtāni yoginaḥ dhyāninaḥ kadā sukha āsane samāsthāya yogī niyata mānasaḥ badhvā kara sampuṭam cam cu ākāreṇa vakreṇa piban vāyum śanais śanais tālu sthā jīva dāyakāḥ tāḥ jighret vāyunā ādāya mṛtam tad śī talaṃjalaṃ kāyaḥ mahā tejāḥ pipāsā kṣudh vivarjitaḥ balena nāgaḥ turagaḥ javena dṛṣṭyā su pūrṇaḥ suśrutiḥ tu dūrāt ākuñcita ākuṃḍali kṛṣṇa keśaḥ gandharva vidyādhara tulya varṇaḥ jīvet naraḥ varpa śatam surāṇām sumedhasā a vākpatinā a sama tvam samākuṃcya abhyaset yogī rasanām tālukam prati kiṃcid kāla antareṇa eva kramāvyāpnoti lambikām mad ayam iva sūkṣmam tatas prasravate sātu saṃspṛṣṭvā śītalām sudhām pivan eva sadā yogī somara tvam hi ganchati repha agram laṃva kāryam padmasya bindu stena aruṣṭam sudhā ogham patati para pade devatā ānanda kāram sāram saṃsāra tāram kṛta kaluṣataram kāraṇam kāla tāram yene mama plāvitām gaṃsa bhavati amaraḥ kṣudh pipāsā vihīnaḥ hi bhavati calaḥ saṃyutaḥ vai hi bhavati calaḥ saṃyutaḥ vai pravakṣye vividham anudinam chāyikam yat śiva ākhyam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām kālajñānam nāma saptacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ kathitaṃ te samāsena chāyikam jñānam uttamam kāmyayā uvāca śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi chāyāpuruṣa lakṣaṇam yam jñātvā puruṣaḥ samyak sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate sūrya hi pṛṣṭhāt kṛtvā maṃbara dharaḥ śukla ambara dharaḥ dhūpa ādi vāsitaḥ nava ātmakam piṇḍa bhūtam svān chāyāḥ sva nirīkṣayet punar ākāśe śveta varṇa svarūpiṇam tat paṭhati eka bhāvaḥ stu śivam parama kāraṇam brahmahatyā ādikaiḥ pāpaiḥ
